European Countries Are Scheming and Secretly Forming Groups 25

Secret Negotiations Are Underway in Capitals of Various Countries

Seeking to Restore the International Balance of Power Before the European War

America's Non-Interference in European Affairs Has Promoted This

France and Germany Each Establish Their Own Factions, Forming Opposition

(London) According to recent news, the secret alliances among European countries are a key to world peace. Secret diplomatic negotiations are currently underway in London, Paris, Berlin, Moscow, Rome, and other places, hoping to create a balance of power. This action is a major reason why American representative Davis announced his non-interference in European affairs after leaving Europe and returning to the United States. Amidst the discussions of disarmament conferences and the reorganization of the League of Nations, the European situation has divided into two factions. One is the connection between Germany, Italy, Austria, and Hungary, with Britain maintaining a semi-neutral position. The other faction is the combination of France, Russia, Poland, Turkey, and other small countries such as Romania, Czechoslovakia, and Yugoslavia.

The small European countries may soon recognize the Soviet Russian government. French Foreign Minister Pengu is traveling to various countries in Eastern Europe and may also go to Russia for contact. As for the background of the development of European countries, there are three main points: (1) German Chancellor Hitler has declared to France that Germany is unwilling to abide by the provisions of the Treaty of Versailles, with a force of 100,000 troops, and the British proposal of 200,000 troops. Germany must have a force of 300,000 troops and 700 military pursuit aircraft, and the Saar region should also be returned to Germany immediately. (2) France has expressed opposition to this proposal. However, if Germany firmly opposes the disarmament conference, France may recognize Germany's demands if it can get help from Britain. (3) British Prime Minister MacDonald spoke with the French ambassador, Tarai, this afternoon, and Tarai is about to return to Paris to report on Britain's attitude. Recently, Britain has been paying close attention to the actions between the Balkan countries, as the Balkan countries are currently engaging in friendly contacts and negotiating non-aggression treaties. (National News Agency dispatch, 25th)

Will Decide After Austria Formally Appeals to the League of Nations

France Fully Expects Britain to Intervene in Germany

How its attitude will be will also depend on the request made by Austria. (Havas dispatch, 25th)

(Paris) The British cabinet expressed its opinion that the major countries related to the German-Austrian issue should persuade Berlin not to engage in activities in Austria before Austria seeks recourse to the League of Nations. Therefore, they want to reunite with Germany and thus want to find a disarmament convention that can reconcile Germany's desire to rearm and France's security concerns. However, Germany's attitude has been firm so far, and it is impossible to reconcile in this way. British cabinet members are careful everywhere to take care of Germany so as not to hurt its feelings. The reason for advocating that countries should persuade Germany before Austria seeks recourse to the League of Nations is to please Germany. The French political circles not only have no reservations about the British cabinet's opinion, but also express their satisfaction with its initiative. If the new British disarmament plan can bring the disarmament convention to a successful conclusion, and if the negotiations with Germany can stop the Hitler Party's activities in Austria, France will be the first to express its happiness. Therefore, people here are paying close attention to the British cabinet's suggestion. However, one thing must be clarified, that is, as of now, London and

Vienna have not notified the French government that they should negotiate with Berlin. (Havas dispatch, 25th)

Japanese Goods Threaten the World Market 41

Lyon Chamber of Commerce Officially Orders International Convention to Ban

New Zealand Authorities Highly Value the Dumping of Japanese Goods

Anglo-Japanese Cotton Industry Negotiations Underway in Lancashire

(Lyon) The local Chamber of Commerce held its first discussion on Japanese business competition and passed a resolution hoping that: (1) an international convention be established to unify the production conditions of all countries without exceptions, and that any country not participating should be subject to a ban on imports from that country by all other signatory nations; (2) before the signing of an international convention, France should limit the quantity of Japanese goods that compete with French products, and the method of limitation should be compatible with Japan's export needs. However, one aspect must be noted: during the European War, all of France's resources were used to defend the country and there was no time for other concerns. Japan seized the opportunity to expand its industrial equipment, and as a result, French commercial markets are now being seized by Japanese goods; (3) the French government should take all kinds of measures to maintain the sales of French goods in colonies and mandated territories. Japanese merchants are increasingly selling goods in French mandated territories without buying return goods; (4) as for Japanese goods that have not yet had quantities limited, and the goods referred to in items two and three, opinions should be solicited from various chambers of commerce in France, and as soon as opinions are collected, the government should take necessary protective measures to maintain the survival of French industry and export trade. (Havas News Agency, 25th)

(London) Lord Panwell, New Zealand's representative in London, told Reuters reporters today that the Japanese threat to New Zealand's commerce is a serious issue. Japan is currently dumping large quantities of goods into New Zealand, and even with high tariffs, it is difficult to compete with its low prices. Therefore, the local government and the British government

are paying close attention to this matter. (Reuters News Agency, 25th)

(London) Minister of Commerce Runciman stayed in Manchester for two days and heard many reproaches, mostly pointing out that the British government had not given sufficient assistance to the Lancashire cotton industry, and had not resisted Japanese competition. However, those in Lancashire who are calm know that the government cannot deal with the overseas Japanese competition in every way, because the cancellation of the Anglo-Japanese commercial treaty would inevitably lead to a fierce trade war between the two countries, and hinder the friendly relations between the two countries. Privately, it is recognized that the Lancashire cotton industry has room for self-help. Indeed, the internal structure of the British cotton industry urgently needs to be reorganized, and old factories that over-invested during the cotton industry boom of 1921 also need to be reorganized. At the same time, the unfair attitude of the French government towards Britain also makes British people very indignant. Britain is France's best customer, but the French import quota for the United States has been restored to its original state due to Washington's negotiations. The original text of the newly established Russo-French commercial treaty, which was published yesterday, also allows Russia to enjoy a quota far exceeding its export volume to France last year. France is only haggling with Britain, and refuses to restore the original quota. French officials admit that they are currently trying to find tools to conduct negotiations on a new Anglo-French commercial treaty, but everyone believes that Britain will never be willing to conduct this negotiation unless the quota reduced by France is fully restored. The British business community now holds a kind of feeling that the principle of treaty-making urgently needs to be revised, and the most-favored-nation clause should be restricted. Although Runciman is doing his best to appease Lancashire's demands, the British Chamber of Commerce has written a letter advocating the adoption of a three-tier tariff system, imposing particularly harsh tariffs on countries that cannot treat Britain fairly. (Reuters News Agency, 26th)

Manchester Minister of Commerce Runciman gave a speech to the Manchester Chamber of Commerce today, mentioning the necessity of dealing with foreign competition, saying that industrialists can rely on the government's continuous assistance in all aspects. Britain's major industries must use the best brains and adopt the most thorough methods of production and distribution, and young talents in universities should engage in commerce instead of doing jobs that are purely parasitic. We oppose foreign political or other forces that may make our competitive efforts come to naught. He knew that the Indo-Japanese cotton spinning agreement was not what Lancashire wanted, but this solution is better than nothing. If the British representatives cannot obtain reasonable conditions from the Japanese side in this Anglo-Japanese negotiation, the British government should help. The Japanese Cotton Industry Committee in Britain has now received long-awaited instructions, instructing them to immediately start negotiations with Lancashire. The Japanese representatives will now contact Lancashire cotton counterparts to discuss the agenda together. (Reuters News Agency, 25th)

Manchester Minister of Commerce Runciman stated today that the Japanese Embassy has stated that there are now various reasons to believe that after the Japanese cotton industry groups obtain the consent of the delegation, the position of Okada and other Japanese representatives can be perfectly defined, and this matter will be discussed when the meeting is held in a few days. Runciman does not agree with artificially encouraging industry, saying that if American methods are applied to the British cotton industry, the result will lead to destruction.

But the British government does not mean that it does not want to provide the cotton industry with the convenience of government organizations. If the British representatives cannot obtain considerable conditions with Japan, then the British government may come forward to help. What we seek is nothing more than a fair method in the world market. Soviet Newspaper Comments on Hirota's Speech 48

Responsibility for Tense Situation in the Far East

Cannot Be Resolved by Flowery Words

Russia's Peaceful Policy Remains Unchanged

(Moscow) Izvestia commented on the speech of the Japanese Foreign Minister Hirota Koki that this speech might have some good influence in improving Japan's international relations, but it cannot be said to have achieved this goal. The formula Hirota used is to attach importance to Japan's national mission in Asia. At the beginning, he stated the perfection of Japan's international relations, and at the end, he said, "Japan's current and future diplomatic relations do have a number of serious problems. Only a prosperous country has a thorny road ahead." On the other hand, Hirota made a statement to the Soviet Union. He wanted to explain that the tension in Japanese-Soviet relations was caused by the change in the Soviet Union's position. Hirota obviously wanted to rely on this statement to reduce the responsibility of the Japanese government for making the situation in the Far East tense. This responsibility should be fully borne by the Japanese government. How can Hirota absolve himself and the Japanese government of responsibility with a few words? As for the Soviet Union, it has proposed the conclusion of a non-aggression pact, agreed to the organization of the Soviet-Japanese-Manchurian border committee, and is willing to sell the Chinese Eastern Railway, which has shown its intention to consolidate peace in the Far East without reservation. The Soviet government's peaceful policy has never changed, and at the same time, if Japan does not finally implement its aggressive plan against the Soviet Union, this policy will not change in the future. It is regrettable that the elements within Japan who support military adventures and plunder are actively pursuing their plan to prepare for this aggression. Unfortunately, Hirota's speech and Hayashi's succession to Araki as Minister of the Army have not shown that the Japanese government has decided not only to eliminate the tense relations between it and the Soviet Union with flowery words, but with concrete facts. This kind of relationship is actually produced by the policy of the Japanese military. (Tass News Agency, 26th)

Chief of Staff of the 29th Army Talks About the Situation of Suppressing Bandits in Sichuan Province 49

(Nanjing) Chengdu, 24th telegram, Gu Zhizhong, head of the Sichuan-Kang investigation group, met with Tang, Chief of Staff of the 29th Army, on the afternoon of the 23rd and talked about the suppression of bandits in detail. According to Tang, at the end of the year before last, Xu Fei, Xiang Qian, and others led a pseudo-Fourth Front Army of about 10,000 people and fled from Shaanxi to Sichuan. Taking advantage of the emptiness of the defenses when the Sichuan war was not yet over, they occupied the three counties of Tongnanba. Tian Songyao, the commander of this army, led his troops to block and suppress them last spring, fought alone, and recovered all the lost land, and was on the verge of extermination. However, due to the sole suppression by one army, it was not easy to encircle, and the economy relied solely on the burdens of the counties in the army's garrison area, and it felt exhausted. When the Sichuan war broke out again, the flames of the bandits took the opportunity to reignite. Tongnanba fell back into the hands of the bandits. Although this army still tried its best to resist and support for ten months, the other armies had no time to take care of it, and the support troops were not dispatched for a while, causing the bandit disaster to spread. Yiyingdaxuan fell one after another. Fortunately, in October, the armies divided up and encircled the bandits, and won victories one after another. Liu Xiang's army recovered Daxuan, Yang Sen's army recovered Yingshan, and this army recovered Yilong. In the past few days, all roads have made great progress. Liu Hanxiong and Wang Zhiyuan's troops of this army occupied Guanyinchang, Liangshuijing, Weijialiang and other places on the 14th. Ye Jishi and He Delong's troops occupied Guanmenshi on the 21st. Luo Naiqiong's division occupied Sanyuanchang on the morning of the 18th. The bandits on the border of Langnan will be eliminated. Li Jiayu's division occupied Yiluchang, and Yang Sen's army occupied Zhuchang. In this way, all roads have made progress. If they can all eliminate private opinions, unite and cooperate, the military affairs of suppressing bandits in Sichuan can be expected to be optimistic. Gu has consulted with the military on a part of the inspection route in Chengdu, and flew east by plane on the morning of the 24th. (Central News Agency, 26th)

(Hankou) Wang Lingji's telegram on the 24th stated that after the recapture of Maduguan, they launched a general attack in three routes, one towards Ruyangyankouchang, one towards Nilongchang Qiujiabao, and one towards Loumenkou Luodawan. The commander of the pseudo-Ninth Army was shot and killed by Xu Fei, and many bandits fled. (Special telegram, 25th)

Kailuan Labor Strike Expands 51

Workers in Four Mines Strike in Succession

Declare Will Not Stop Until Goal is Achieved

Mine Owner Declares No Responsibility

British Consulate Asks Authorities to Stop Quickly

(Tianjin) On the 25th, workers in Tangjiazhuang, Kailuan, and on the 26th, workers in Linxi and Tangshan mines went on strike to support the workers in Majiagou mine, demanding five conditions from the mine owner: 1. Restore the labor union; 2. Dissolve the mine area security team and punish the perpetrators; 3. All unemployed workers will be reinstated; 4. Provide compensation to the deceased workers; 5. Abolish the contract system. Workers in the three mines declared that they would never return to work until the goal is achieved. Today, the person in charge of the Kailuan Mining Bureau said that of the five mines, only Zhaogezhuang mine is still working. Since the strike on the 21st, the mining side has suffered too much loss. The mining side has made up its mind to endure the pain and seek a quick end to the strike, and the workers return to the mine to work, but it has not worked. This strike is definitely not a labor-capital dispute as rumored, because since the workers went on strike, no one has come to the mine to demand an increase in any treatment. As for the workers' request to restore the labor union, it is not the responsibility of the mining side. (Special telegram, 26th)

(Tianjin) In the Kailuan coal mine turmoil, the conditions between labor and capital have not been agreed upon, and the workers are still continuing their strike. This afternoon, British Consul-General in Tianjin, Zhai Lansi, and Nason Edward, Kailuan Mining Director, went to the Provincial Government to meet and ask to severely punish the instigators of the strike and force the workers to resume work. Yu did not agree, saying that he had ordered the real hall to send staff to the mine to adopt peaceful methods and advise the workers not to insist on the labor union organization and resume work first. (Special telegram, 26th)

(Tianjin) The Kailuan coal mine strike turmoil has been expanding since the 14th. There are a total of five mines in Kailuan, namely (1) Majiagou (2) Zhaogezhuang, (3) Linxi, (4) Tangjiazhuang, (5) Tangshan. The first to launch this strike was Majiagou. The two sides have been deadlocked for more than ten days. Unexpectedly, the workers in the Linxi mine area suddenly continued their strike on the 25th. On the same night, the workers in Tangjiazhuang also went on strike one after another. On the morning of the 26th, Zhaogezhuang also showed signs of strike. The workers in the Tangshan mine area also stated that if there is no practical solution within three days, all the workers will act in unison. It is heard that the point of contention in this strike is to restore the labor union. According to the Bureau, this kind of authority is not within the Bureau, because the Tanggu Agreement restricts the activities of labor unions within the war zone, so the Bureau is unable to be responsible for the strike. The British Consul and the manager of the mine visited Chairman Yu at 6 pm on the 26th, asking him to pay attention and ask for a quick solution. (Central News Agency, 26th)

Course of the Central Army's Recovery of Zhangzhou 89

The Third Division Lands in Song and Advances on Zhang

The 19th Route Army Retreats Without a Fight

A dispatch from Xiamen states that Cai Tingkai left the province on the 15th and flew to Zhangzhou to command the 60th Division of Shen Guanghan, the 78th Division of Qu Shounian, the 49th Division of Zhang Yan, and other units totaling more than 20,000 troops, who retreated south from Fuzhou. They were deployed between Xianyou and Putian. The Central Army, with ten divisions (a total of twelve divisions of the Central Army entering Fujian, plus about two divisions of the Zhejiang Security Force and special forces, for a total strength of fourteen divisions), advanced south in two routes. The Fourth and Tenth Divisions crossed the river at Shuikou on the 17th and advanced towards Xianyou via Yongtai. The Thirty-sixth and Ninth Divisions crossed the river at Xiadou in the provincial capital on the morning of the 18th and advanced towards Putian via Fuqing, advancing very rapidly. It was hoped that they would strike the retreating troops of the 19th Route Army before their defenses were established. The Fourth and Tenth Divisions reached Xianyou on the 19th, and the Ninth and Thirty-sixth Divisions reached Putian on the 20th. The 19th Route Army had not originally planned to retreat to southern Fujian, so there were no preparations made in advance between Putian and Xianyou. At this time, the ranks were in disarray, and the Central Army pursued closely until the area between Putian and Xianyou, and the Shaxi Yiban area between Huian and Fengting, where the 19th Route Army began to establish defenses based on the natural terrain and counterattack. The troops of the four divisions of the Central Army on both routes converged and attacked from three sides. Fierce fighting began on the 20th. Cai Tingkai commanded at the front, and the troops collapsed again on the morning of the 21st. In this battle, the Central Army captured more than 6,000 rifles, hundreds of light and heavy machine guns, dozens of various artillery pieces, and more than 20 vehicles, and captured more than 6,000 prisoners. The defeated soldiers abandoned their weapons along the way, and the Huian militia and villagers picked up no less than several thousand more. The Thirty-sixth Division took advantage of the victory to pursue and occupied Huian County on the afternoon of the 21st. The vanguard reached Luoyang Bridge that evening. On the 22nd, most of the troops continued to arrive, but because Shen Guanghan and others telegraphed from Quanzhou to declare their allegiance, they were ordered to temporarily stop the pursuit. Currently, the Thirty-sixth and Ninth Divisions are temporarily stationed in the southern part of Luoyang. This is the battle situation of the Central Army's southward pursuit of the Putian-Xianyou area.

The biggest reason for the defeat of the 19th Route Army after its retreat to the south was that Zhangzhou was attacked by the Central Army's Third Division, which landed in Songyu by sea from Xiamen on the morning of the 20th. The loss of Zhangzhou meant that the rear was completely cut off, and they were trapped in a pincer attack from both Putian-Xianyou and Zhangzhou, with no way to retreat. Cai Tingkai planned to cede the defense of Zhangzhou and Longyan to the Guangdong Army in order to secure his rear, while using the remaining 40,000 troops to defend Quanzhou and Zhangzhou to the death. However, when the war in northern Fujian began, most of the troops in southern Fujian were transferred to the province, leaving only the 49th Division's Zhou Lixing regiment of Zhang Yan's department, as well as two artillery battalions and six to seven hundred students from the military academy in Zhangzhou. As a result, when the Central Army's Third Division landed in Songyu and advanced on Zhangzhou, Xu Minghong, who was in Zhangzhou, knew that it could not be defended and ordered the abandonment of Zhangzhou and retreat on the afternoon of the 20th. By the morning of the 21st, they had retreated completely towards Longyan. When Shen Mao and others in Quanzhou learned that Zhangzhou had been lost, they issued a telegram on the afternoon of the 21st declaring their allegiance.

The Central Army that recovered Zhangzhou and Tong'an was the Eighth and Ninth Brigades of the Third Division and the Fifteenth, Sixteenth, and Supplemental Regiments of the Fourth Column of the Northern Route Bandit Suppression Army, commanded by Division Commander Li Yutang and Deputy Division Commander Yang Tingya. On the 19th, they sailed from the province via Taishun, Xinning, Xing, Hai'an, Xinming, Yunlong, Fengpu, and Liulun, and arrived in Xiamen on the morning of the 20th, landing in Songyu. The several dozen members of the Fujian Western Volunteer Corps stationed in Songyu retreated along the Zhangzhou-Songyu highway towards Zhangzhou upon seeing the arrival of the large army. The Supplemental Regiment of the Third Division, led by Bian Ling, pursued, and the Volunteer Corps retreated while fighting. After Xiamen was recovered, the transportation between Zhangzhou and Xiamen was cut off. Xu Minghong, the puppet governor of Longyan Province, and Yu Huamu, the garrison commander of Zhangzhou, Longyan, and Xiamen, in order to maintain the morale of the people in Zhangzhou, confiscated and burned all Xiamen newspapers transported to Zhangzhou, even those sent by mail. The peasant association between Zhangzhou and Xiamen was very active, and they often shot those they identified as local tyrants. On the 15th, Xu Minghong also published a small one-page public newspaper, carrying news from their side. On the morning of the 20th, Xu Minghong received news that the Central Army had landed in Songyu and decided to abandon Zhangzhou and retreat to Longyan. On one hand, he sent a team to the Longxi Chamber of Commerce to demand 30,000 yuan, surrounding the chamber of commerce as if facing a formidable enemy, and finally took away 15,000 yuan. In Zhao'an, Zhang Shiyu, commander of the Fourth Detachment of Yang Fengnian's Southern Fujian Anti-Rebel Army, led Shen Donghai in capturing Zhao'an, Dongshan, and Yunxiao, and then attacked Zhangpu. At the same time, the militia between Zhangzhou, Xiamen, and Haicheng rose up. In addition to dispatching a battalion of Zhou's regiment to defend Zhangpu, Xu Minghong also deployed more than 1,600 volunteer troops reorganized from the Communist Red Guards to defend the Zhangzhou, Xiamen, and Haicheng area to maintain local order. Later, with the loss of Zhangzhou, they also collapsed and retreated. Before the 19th Route Army abandoned Zhangzhou, they first ordered all troops and personnel of various agencies in the city to retreat by 5:00 a.m. on the 21st. However, the matter happened suddenly, just like the unprepared abandonment of Fuzhou. As a result, all guns, ammunition, and military rice were difficult to transport together. In addition, most of the vehicles in Zhangzhou were driven to northern Fujian, and many are still in the Putian-Xianyou area, so there were no vehicles available for transport. At 2:40 a.m. on the 21st, the gunpowder depot next to the West Gate County Government, Madudi, the Li Ancestral Hall, the arsenal, and the ordnance depot of the 49th Division in Dagouqian, the ordnance depot of the 60th Division at the mouth of the County Government, and the ordnance and baggage depot of the Zhishan Barracks were burned at the same time. For a time, the sound of explosions and gunfire was deafening throughout the city. At the Zhangpu station, the troops sealed the cars because no one answered the door when they knocked, and they were also burned. At dawn, the residents learned that the troops had retreated and rushed out to loot the military equipment, ammunition, and tools from the military and political agencies. The whole city was in a state of anarchy. Several people were shot dead during the competition for weapons and ammunition. The 19th Route Army retreated towards Nanjing. Those who retreated included 600 to 700 students from the Zhishan Military Officer Training Class, more than 1,500 infantrymen from the Zhou Lixing regiment of the 49th Division, one artillery battalion of the Fourth Army, one artillery battalion of the Third Division, more than 100 members of the County Government Security Team, Xu Minghong's political security division, and staff members of the rear office, the Peasants' Liberation Association, the General Labor Union, and special commissioners from various districts, totaling about 4,000 people. After arriving in Nanjing, they retreated to the depths. At about 10:00, Chen Linrong, commander of the Sixth Detachment of the Anti-Rebel Army, and Zhang Longqing, commander of the Fourth Regiment, each led a large team of about 300 to 400 people into the city. After entering the city, Zhang found hidden weapons of the 19th Route Army in a civilian house on Zhishan Kou Main Street, including more than 2,000 newly manufactured 1933 American rapid-fire rifles, 13 anti-aircraft machine guns, and other military supplies, which were all carried away by Zhang's troops.

In addition, the military equipment and ammunition of the 19th Route Army stored in Nanxiang were also carried away by Zhang Feiji, a member of the militia. Therefore, the failure of the 19th Route Army this time was due to the lack of combat preparedness. The number of guns lost below Yanping and recovered by the militia is unknown. This is a major problem for the post-war settlement in Fujian. At about 1:00 p.m. on the 21st, the Central Army arrived in Zhangzhou and dropped a bomb in Madudi that did not explode. The Chamber of Commerce urgently notified the whole city to hang the Blue Sky White Sun flag. At 5:00 a.m. on the 22nd, all the supplemental regiments of the Central Army's Third Division, led by Regiment Commander Fan Ling, arrived in Zhangzhou, thus completely recovering Zhangzhou. Division Commander Li Yutang arrived in Zhangzhou at 1:00 p.m. on the 22nd. Part of the Ninth Brigade continued to enter Zhangzhou in the afternoon, totaling about 3,000 people. In addition, on the 21st, the province continued to transport the 17th and 18th Regiments of the Third Division to Xiamen for landing. In addition to the two regiments heading to Zhangzhou, the remaining Eighth and Ninth Brigade Headquarters and the four regiments of the 15th, 16th, 17th, and 18th Regiments all transferred to Tong'an via Jiaowei.

In Tong'an, there was originally only one battalion of Yun's regiment of the 19th Route Army stationed. In addition, there was Chen Wenzong, the commander of the Zhangzhou-Longyan guerrilla force appointed by the 19th Route Army, who also served as the county magistrate. At noon on the 20th, Yun's battalion was ordered to concentrate and retreat. On the 21st, Chen Wenzong declared his allegiance and was appointed as the commander of the Ninth Detachment of the Anti-Rebel Army by Du Qiyun. At 10:00 p.m. that night, the 15th and 16th Regiments of the Third Division arrived at the county seat from Jiaowei via Guankou. Because the password did not match, they were attacked by the troops, killing two members of Chen's unit and confiscating more than 20 weapons. Chen's unit retreated to outside the city. On the morning of the 22nd, the 17th and 18th Regiments of the Third Division continued to arrive in Tong'an. The vanguard of the Third Division advanced to Maxiang. The Eighth and Ninth Brigade Headquarters, totaling about 10,000 people, were all stationed in Tong'an County. After Li Yutang arrived in Zhangzhou, he returned to Tong'an on the morning of the 23rd to command the troops and contact a certain division of the Central Army advancing towards Xiwei and Anxi. His division headquarters was set up in Zhangzhou.

Jiang Dingwen, the Commander-in-Chief of the Northern Route Bandit Suppression Army, arrived in Xiamen on the 21st to preside over the military affairs in southern Fujian. On the 22nd, he established the General Headquarters at the Xiamen Public Security Bureau (the Public Security Bureau moved back to Huanzhu Hall). All the personnel of the General Headquarters arrived in Xiamen on the 23rd and began to work immediately. When Jiang arrived in Xiamen, Shen Guanghan, Mao Weishou, Qu Shounian, and Zhang Yan sent out telegrams from Quanzhou declaring their allegiance. After receiving the telegram, Jiang telegraphed Chairman Chiang for instructions and ordered the various armies to continue their military operations according to the original orders. (23rd)

Ma Zhanshan Decides to Go Abroad 90

First to the Philippines, then to the Americas

Planning to Study Industries for Half a Year

According to a dispatch from Tianjin, the news that Ma Zhanshan is going abroad is confirmed. However, the date of departure is still uncertain. Those close to Ma said that Ma suffered greatly from stimulation after returning home from Europe. He suffers from neurasthenia and stomach problems. Last week, his condition worsened and he was bedridden for several days. Later, two famous acupuncturists were invited from Beiping for diagnosis and treatment, and he was finally cured. Someone recently saw Ma, who was unusually thin and coughed frequently. When discussing the current situation and national affairs, he remained silent. His going abroad is said to be entirely voluntary. He feels that he has become useless since returning home, and the outside world has taken advantage of his seclusion to fabricate rumors. Some people said that Ma was colluding with frustrated warlords and politicians to plan a different movement, and others said that Ma was joining hands with the Japanese to start a new situation in North China. At the same time, the Japanese side is also paying close attention to Ma's actions. Half a month ago, before Sun Dianying invaded the west, he once instructed his staff office, saying that Ma Zhanshan had arrived in Woye and joined the army to cooperate. Sun deliberately spread rumors in order to boost military morale by using Ma's reputation. After the rumors spread, the military and political authorities in North China paid close attention to them and sent representatives to Tianjin to visit Ma and observe his movements. Ma firmly stayed at home and did not leave his door. The representatives returned to Beiping and reported, and the general doubts began to be resolved. Ma decided to take a trip abroad unexpectedly due to the poor domestic environment, partly to avoid the proliferation of rumors and partly to broaden his horizons. Therefore, he specifically telegraphed the Nanchang headquarters to Chiang, requesting permission to travel abroad and was replied with a telegram of approval and an allocation of 30,000 yuan for travel expenses. Ma originally planned to travel before the Chinese New Year, but it was delayed due to illness. It was changed to late February after the Spring Festival. Three attendants were appointed. Before going abroad, he will go to Shanghai to apply for a passport and receive travel expenses. He plans to go to the Philippines first for a short stay, and then go to North and South America to study the military equipment and industries of those regions, preparing to return home and enter the industrial sector. The return trip is expected to take half a year. If time permits, he will also visit Honolulu. Ma's former subordinates, who are stranded in Beiping and have not yet been settled, include 51 officers and 63 junior officers. He had previously submitted a request to the central government for relief and received a reply approving the review and ordering the Beiping branch of the Military Commission to pay 50,000 yuan at one time. Some of the officers and junior officers will be employed by the Military Commission. Ma specially appointed former Heilongjiang Civil Affairs Commissioner Lang Guanshan and Chief of Staff Rong Yuan to handle the matter in Beiping. It is said that each officer can receive 400 yuan, and each junior officer can receive more than 300 yuan. The families of the fallen soldiers will be compensated according to the circumstances. (24th)

Japanese Fishing Boats Invade Shandong's Inland Harbors 91

Shandong Provincial Government Consults Ministry of Foreign Affairs for Just Negotiations

According to a dispatch from Jinan, the Shandong Yellow River coastal area, Yantai, Weihai, Rongcheng Bay, Dingzi Bay, and Jiaozhou Bay are all good harbors, possessing the advantages of both fishing and salt production, and are the foundation of the livelihood of the coastal people. However, due to the weakness of our country's naval forces, bandits come and go at will, hindering the livelihood of fishermen, and the Japanese are even more keen on spying and coveting. Therefore, Japanese fishing boats often invade our territorial waters, vying for our rights and interests. Some time ago, Rongcheng County Chief Zhou Baoli reported to the province that Japanese fishing boats had invaded the port of Shidao. Because the seawater had frozen, the fishing nets were frozen together and could not be moved. They landed on the beach by sampan and went to Xilan Village to find people to help them cut off the fishing nets so that they could return home. Jiang Xijin, the director of the Shidao Public Security Bureau, went to investigate and learned that the fishing boat was named the Third Irigayemaru, carrying five Japanese fishermen, and had sailed from Dalian. After cutting off the fishing nets, they sailed out of Shidao. County Chief Zhou Baoli of the county reported that the Japanese fishing boats had freely invaded our inland harbors to catch fish, which was a violation of our territorial sovereignty. Moreover, the fishing boat was a gasoline boat, and the sound of its sputtering reverberated for several miles, blocking the fish schools and preventing them from returning. As a result, the amount of fish produced along the coast each year has been decreasing, which has a profound impact on our country's fishing industry and the livelihoods of fishermen. Therefore, he specifically requested the provincial government to forward a letter to the Japanese consul, asking him to strictly prohibit this and guarantee that such incidents would not happen again in the future. Based on this, the provincial government submitted it to the political affairs meeting yesterday to discuss solutions. It was decided to consult the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for handling. (24th)

Supervisory Yuan's Impeachment of Wang Zhengting 92

Wang Abused Power and Sold Out Overseas Chinese While Foreign Minister

Punishment Committee Resolves to Suspend Him from Office for Five Years

The National Government's Committee for the Punishment of Political Officials, acting on a previous order from the National Government regarding the case of former Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting's disloyalty to the Party, dereliction of duty, abuse of power, humiliation of the nation, selling out overseas Chinese, and currying favor with foreigners, which was brought forward by Supervisory Committee member Zheng Luosheng through impeachment, and after review by the Supervisory Yuan, found the evidence to be conclusive and that the impeached Wang Zhengting should be handed over for punishment. It is reported that after receiving the order, the committee resolved on November 2 of last year that Wang Zhengting's impeachment was based on established facts and that he should be punished with a five-year suspension from office as a form of reprimand. The Supervisory Yuan's original report to the National Government is recorded below: "Reporting on the matter of requesting handover for punishment in accordance with the law. According to Supervisory Committee member Zheng Luosheng's proposal, regarding the Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting's recognition of the Malayan government's suppression of the Chinese Kuomintang's Malayan General Branch, he acted deceitfully and is hereby impeached based on the facts. The committee returned to China on August 25 of last year and reported to the Central Party Headquarters regarding fundraising for rear-area hospitals for disaster relief in the Northwest, which was stopped by the Star Governor Jin Wentai, and he was expelled from the country. It was submitted to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for handling. (Original text omitted.) Looking at Wang Zhengting's various acts of disloyalty to the Party, dereliction of duty, abuse of power, humiliation of the nation, selling out overseas Chinese, and currying favor with foreigners, he should be impeached in accordance with the law. Is this appropriate? We humbly request that it be handed over for review in accordance with the law. One copy of the attachment is submitted herewith." After assigning Supervisory Committee members Xie Wuliang, Luo Jiefu, and Gao Youtang to review it, we now report that, based on the case handed down by Committee member Zheng Luosheng impeaching Foreign Minister Wang Wangting, the committee members' review concluded that the minister's disloyalty to the Party, dereliction of duty, and abuse of power were supported by conclusive evidence and that the impeached person should be handed over for punishment. Based on this, we hereby submit the original attachments and request your government to review and implement them. Respectfully submitted, one.

Songjiang

Small-Scale Silk Shop Goes Bankrupt 93

Since cheap silk fabrics were sold at stalls in this city since the spring, customers flocked to them, and their business surpassed that of the established silk shops. As a result, the stalls gradually changed their scale and expanded their scope, with capital generally ranging from two to three thousand yuan. Shops lined up along Malu Bridge, and the silk fabric industry began to be divided into large and small businesses. Now, Yuan Da Silk Shop, which opened in Guanyi Post, suddenly went bankrupt, reportedly owing more than 10,000 yuan, with only about 3,000 yuan in inventory. The manager, Lu Bogeng, has now hired lawyer Zhang Zhijie to handle the liquidation. The Shanghai silk shops that are owed the most have also sent personnel to Songjiang to hire lawyer Gu Shouyi to handle the pursuit of legal proceedings. All the inventory has now been sent to the county chamber of commerce for sealing and storage, to be used for future compensation.

Fire Accident at the Wang Residence in Xiaocang Bridge 94

At the Wang Yougen residence in Xiaocang Tu, outside the West Gate, today (26th) was the occasion of his young son's transfer to a foster family, and relatives and friends gathered for a banquet. Unexpectedly, at around 3 p.m., a fire suddenly broke out in the firewood room of the fifth courtyard. After it was discovered, gongs were sounded to raise the alarm. The West Section Fire Brigade was the first to drive its dragon cart to the scene to put out the fire. Next to the firewood room was the bedroom, and the firefighters climbed onto the roof to dismantle it, so the flames were prevented from spreading, and fortunately, it was preserved.

Wujiang

All Waterway Transportation in This County is Blocked 95

All districts in this county rely on boats for transportation. Due to the severe cold weather in recent days, the river water has frozen, and the boats have stopped running. Waterway transportation has been completely halted for five days. Fortunately, the long-distance buses on the Sujia Road can pass through the urban area, Bachi, Pingwang, and Shengze, so transportation is still relatively convenient. However, there are quite a few passengers traveling back and forth, and the vehicles are insufficient, so each bus is extremely crowded.

Wuxi

Bandit Li Zhiping Executed 96

In the case of Han Wentai, the head of Xiexie Township in the Third District (Yangming Township), who was kidnapped by bandits last spring, Wu Zhengrong, the chief of political affairs of the county government, and Xue Furi, the captain of the detective team of the Public Security Bureau, led detectives to arrest the bandits involved in the case, Li Zhiping, Jiang Hanchen, Yang Abao, Zhou Shungen, and Luo Sanxing, one after another in Suzhou, Wuxi, and Shanghai. The cases of Li and Jiang were handled by the county court, while the cases of Yang, Zhou, and Luo were handled by the county government. On the 17th of this month, the county government obtained approval from the provincial government to execute Yang and Zhou by shooting first, while Luo Sanxing is still in custody awaiting decision. The county court also sentenced Li and Jiang to death and submitted them to the province for review. Later, the provincial government sent the case of Jiang Hanchen back to the original court for retrial, while Li Zhiping was approved for execution. At 1 p.m. yesterday, the county court received the order from the Higher Court forwarded by the province. The prosecutor Ren, together with the warden Sun Gongwu, took their seats in the courtroom and ordered the police to bring the prisoner Li to the court to verify his identity. He was then taken to the South Training Ground and executed by shooting. Prosecutor Ren served as the supervising officer, and Chief Zhou also showed up to announce the charges.

Dafengsheng Rice Shop Grounded 97

Dafengsheng Rice Shop, located in the Beitang Coal Yard Alley, has been open for many years and is a large-scale operation. On ordinary days, merchants from Jintan, Liyang, Tianjin, Fujian, Zhejiang, Chuzhou, Wuyi, and Liuhe gather here, and business is extremely prosperous. It can be said to be the leader of the rice industry in the county. The owner of the shop, Xu Xiezhang, also serves as the manager, but the actual power of all silver and money transactions is in the hands of the chief accountant, Gong Fengming. In recent years, the market price of rice and grain has plummeted, and the shop has suffered heavy losses year after year. Because Gong Fengming's methods were agile, he could barely maintain it at first, but by last month, it finally became unsustainable. Gong Fengming quietly absconded with 800 yuan, and the shop was stranded. In total, it owes various banks, money shops, warehouses, and customer deposits about 100,000 yuan. The creditors from the silver money industry and the storage industry, seeing that Dafengsheng's liquidation was indefinite, planned to sell the customer goods stored in various warehouses on behalf of the customers to repay the debts. However, after hearing the news, the merchants, whose capital was at stake, jointly sent a letter to the county chamber of commerce, asking it to uphold justice and forward the letter to the silver money and storage industry to temporarily retain the goods. A small number of merchant creditors flocked to Dafengsheng to demand payment of their debts, but to no avail.

Suzhou

Completion of the County's Road Network 98

In the past three years, the construction projects in Wu County have focused on road construction. County Magistrate Zou Jing has now proposed a plan to complete the county's road network. In addition to connecting the neighboring counties of Suxi, Suchang, Sukun, Suwu, and Sulu, five trunk roads, some of which have already been completed, there are more than 20 branch roads that run through the various rural areas in the east, south, west, and north. Yesterday (26th), they were submitted and passed at the county administrative meeting. They will be built gradually, prioritizing those with greater urgency. In the future, after the western road network is completed, Mudu can be used as a scenic area to organize the Lingyan, Tianping, and Shihu landscapes to attract foreign tourists and revitalize the rural areas.

Trial Scheduled for Seventy-Year-Old Man Accused of Abandonment 99

Xu Yuanxiu, a Chinese secretary at Soochow University, is seventy years old. His first wife, Xu Ge, whom he abandoned in the countryside forty years ago, hired lawyer Liu Zuwang to sue him in the Wu County District Court, demanding alimony. The case was mediated by someone, but now that the mediation has failed, the court has scheduled the trial for the afternoon of February 22.

Vendetta Murder Case Occurs in Yudong 100

Li Yuxing's house in Yudong District, Nantong, was suddenly invaded by thugs who shot and killed Li and also wounded his son, Li Fuen, with a knife. The Public Security Bureau has been notified to investigate and arrest the murderers.

Jiangyin

Dredging of the Dongheng River to be Implemented 102

The Dongheng River was dredged in 1915. After twenty years, the county government has deliberated on the dredging, designed a plan, and submitted it to the Construction Department for approval. It has been decided to breach the dam on February 1, lower the water level on the 20th, and start dredging on March 20. The general office of the entire river project will be located in Zhanwen Bridge. The method of starting work will follow the old regulations of labor provided in lieu of food by tenants.

Zhenjiang

Rickshaw Pullers Petition Again 103

On the 23rd of last month, the rickshaw pullers in Zhenjiang went on strike because they demanded a reduction in rickshaw rental fees. Later, the military and police authorities stopped them, and after explanations from all parties concerned, no incident occurred. The rickshaw pullers were disappointed with their previous demands. In addition, the weather was cold and the end of the year was approaching, and the market was sluggish. Many of them could hardly feed their families after paying the rickshaw rental fees. After the Zhenjiang Railway Station on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway and the Zhenyang Automobile Company implemented joint transportation, business became even more slack. In order to maintain their livelihood, more than a hundred rickshaw pullers elected representatives and gathered at the West Railway Station yesterday morning, holding banners and parading in formation. At 10 a.m., they went to the chamber of commerce to request relief and reportedly demanded three things: (1) Cancel the joint transportation between the Beijing-Shanghai Railway and the Zhenyang Automobile Company; (2) Reduce rickshaw rental fees; (3) Request the winter relief bureau to increase the distribution of rice porridge to rickshaw pullers. The person who received them promised to do everything possible to find a solution. The rickshaw pullers then withdrew. In the afternoon, more than a thousand people gathered at the county sports field, intending to petition the provincial party and government organs again, but they dispersed after being persuaded by the military and police.

Jiaxing

Demolition of the Remaining City Walls Begins 104

The Jiaxing city walls from the south city eastward to the north city have long been demolished. However, the remaining city walls from the Lotus Dike in the north city westward to the Chenghai Bridge in the south gate have been contracted for demolition by the county government in order to completely build the ring road around the city. The Hua Cheng Construction Company has won the bid for this project and started demolition the day before yesterday. All buildings, plants, and temporary graves within the road alignment area have been ordered by the county government to be moved and removed within a limited time to facilitate the project. If the deadline is exceeded, the county will hire workers to move and remove them on their behalf, and the wages will still be paid by the owners. The demolition and relocation fees and land prices will be collected from the county construction department in accordance with the precedent set during the second phase of the demolition of the city and road construction.

Jiashan

Measures for Tax Collection on Land with Grain Shortages 105

The County Finance Bureau has received instructions from the Provincial Finance and Civil Affairs Departments regarding land with grain shortages. Before the survey and measurement are completed or if they have started but not finished, those who report to the bureau to make up for the grain shortage will be allowed to complete it for one year. If they deliberately delay reporting and are discovered later, they will be handled as overflow land or lost grain land, and they must pay three years of grain tax and register to bear the grain burden. The grain tax collected for one year or three years will be allocated to survey and measurement expenses. This measure has been resolved at the 647th meeting of the Provincial Government Conference and is hereby ordered to all counties. The County Finance Bureau has followed it after receiving the order.

The New Aircraft of the China Aviation Company Will Arrive Tomorrow

Commemoration Meeting for the Second Anniversary of the "January 28th" Incident to be Held by All Sectors 110

Scheduled to be Held at the City Chamber of Commerce at 9 a.m.

The Entire City Will Fly Flags at Half-Mast and the Military and Police Will Work Overtime to Maintain Alert

January 28 is the anniversary of the Songhu Anti-Japanese War. The people of all sectors of this city have scheduled a commemoration meeting to be held at the City Chamber of Commerce at 9 a.m. on that day. The entire city will fly flags at half-mast and will step up security for the day. Details are recorded below.

Meeting Order

The City Party Headquarters has already drafted the order of the commemoration meeting as follows: (1) Opening; (2) Singing the Party song; (3) Paying the highest respect to the Party and National Flag and the portrait of the Premier; (4) Reading the Premier's will; (5) Silent tribute; (6) Chairman's report; (7) Speeches; (8) Shouting slogans; (9) Conclusion. As for the chairman of the meeting, he will be nominated by the executive and supervisory committee members.

Party Headquarters Notice

The City Party Headquarters issued a notice to all agencies, schools, and groups participating in the commemoration, saying, "For the matter of notification, since January 28 is the anniversary of the Songhu Anti-Japanese War, this association has scheduled a meeting to be held at 9 a.m. on that day in the auditorium of the City Chamber of Commerce to convene representatives from all walks of life for a commemoration meeting. Special notification is hereby given. It is hoped that all agencies, schools, groups, and party headquarters at all levels in this city will send two representatives each, with a letter of participation as required. Special notification is hereby given."

Citywide Security

On the second anniversary of "January 28," all sectors of this city consider the Songhu bloody battle to be the most deeply painful war. In order to mourn the martyred soldiers and the compatriots who were killed, it was decided that the entire city would fly flags at half-mast on that day to express grief. The city police and military authorities, fearing that reactionary elements would take the opportunity to cause trouble, decided to simultaneously step up security for the day. The City Public Security Bureau also ordered all district offices to work overtime to strengthen prevention, and all detectives, inspectors, and male and female investigators were dispatched to simultaneously stop illegal marches and gatherings in order to maintain security.

Rent Reduction Association Held Representative Assembly Yesterday 111

Approved Various Important Cases on Rent Reduction Principles

Russian Merchants Association Joins in Unified Action

The Shanghai Rent Reduction Movement Association previously drafted rent reduction principles by the executive committee on the previous day. Yesterday at 2 p.m., it convened a joint meeting of representatives from various groups in the regular meeting room of the City Chamber of Commerce to discuss them in detail and has approved them. The details are recorded on the left.

Representatives Present

Yesterday, representatives from the following groups attended the meeting: Zhang Yichen from the Citizens' General Union, Zhang Xilin from the Chicken and Duck Industry Guild, Sun Qiuping from the Hotel Industry Association, Dong Menghuang from the Candle Industry Guild, Luo Haitao from the Noodle Shop Industry Guild, Shi Hongxun from the Rice Shop Industry Guild, Yuan Hongjun from the Leather Shoe Nail Industry Guild, Ye Jiaxing from the Sausage Industry Guild, Wang Honghui from the Chemical Raw Materials Industry Guild, Mao Xinpu from the Machine-Made Noodle Cutting Industry Guild, Luo Zheng from the New-Style Laundry Industry Guild, Shu Huizhen from the Women's Patriotic Goods Promotion Association, Hong Songtong from the Flower and Tree Industry Guild, Ka Xingyuan from the Foshan Dyeing Industry Guild, Zhou Fuzhang, Cai Qiajun, Qiu Jialiang, Chen Jiufeng, Liu Zhongying, Zheng Baohua, Shen Hefu, Zhao Erchang, Fei Liangheng, Zhu Zhichun, Zheng Xiaolin, Zhang Chizeng, Yu Hualong, Chen Jicheng, Zhang Dafu, Ge Futian, and other representatives from various district citizens' associations and various hometown associations, totaling more than a hundred people.

Resolutions

Zhang Yichen, Ye Jiaxing, Zhang Xianfang, and Cao Zhigong were elected as the presidium, and Zheng Dongshan recorded the minutes. After the formalities were completed, the chairman gave a report, (1) reporting on the principles of the association's meeting and the subsequent plan of action, (2) motions from the previous representative assembly's executive committee and standing committee, which have been reported in the newspapers, (3) letters from various parties, (A) Hubei District Rent Reduction Association Delin Lane Branch, (B) Renheli Rent Reduction Association Branch, (C) Shoupinli Rent Reduction Association Branch, (D) Russian Merchants Association, etc., joining the association, matters for discussion, (1) the association's organizational system method case, resolved, (A) establish district branches according to the citizen association format, with branches under the district branches, (B) add an investigation section to each department, (C) both Chinese and foreigners enjoy the right to rent reduction in this city, (D) communications, etc., should be handed over to the executive committee, and special committees may be established, (2) how to increase the number of alternate members on the executive committee, resolved, (A) revise the rules and add eleven alternate members (list to be recorded separately), (3) rent reduction principles, approved item by item, resolved, (1) houses built in 1924 pay rent at 90% of the original rent, (2) 80% of the original rent for 1925-1927, (3) 70% of the original rent for 1928-1930, (A) 60% of the original rent for 1931-1933, based on the current rent charged, if the rent has been increased, calculate based on the date the house was built, (4) if elected members should be asked to attend meetings due to the intensity of work, resolved,

(A) Members who do not attend twice will be warned (B) Those who do not attend three times will be replaced by alternate members, to be executed by the executive committee, (5) announcement of rent reduction principles to landlords, resolved, passed, (6) what to do if landlords do not accept the reduced rent, resolved, deposit the actual rent in a bank and register the receipt or passbook with the association, announce it to the landlord, if they do not handle it according to the law, the association cannot guarantee anything, (7) rent reduction, sub-landlords and third-tier tenants receive equal treatment, resolved, passed (provided that third-tier tenants pay off rent owed before 1934), (8) hold a large-scale petition when necessary for the rent reduction movement, resolved, passed.

Temporary Motions

(A) The Shoupinli and other rent reduction movement branches proposed that landlords have expanded rent increases and are forcing people to move out within a limited time, and want to cut off water, etc., should be asked for assistance, resolved, (1) a separate committee will be formed to handle rent increases, and the executive committee will discuss the principles, (2) January 28 is the general mobilization day for rent reduction, resolved, (A) distribute slogans and leaflets, (B) the publicity department will handle publicity matters in order to make it universal.

Increased Number of Alternate Members

The association previously designated members, with warning measures for non-attendance, and specially added eleven alternate members: Shi Hongxun, Yu Zhongxian, Zhou Fuzhang, Qiu Jialiang, Sun Qiuping, Sun Choucheng, Luo Zheng, Lu Rongling, Zhao Erchang, Hu Yibo, Ren Nongxuan, and others.

We hope to hear back as soon as possible." Chairman of the Russian Merchants Association, Aikibonowski.

Landlords and Tenants Should Seek Mutual Consideration

The Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce held its 14th Executive Committee meeting yesterday, attended by Wang Xiaolai, Wang Yansong, Bei Songsun, Yu Zuoting, Lu Wenshao, Wen Lanting, Ma Jiliang, and others, more than twenty people. Since the "January 28" battle, Shanghai has not recovered. In March of this year, various industries had a rent reduction movement and sent a letter to this association, requesting assistance.
