Shen Bao Wireless Weekly

Two Important Questions Regarding Crystal Radios 154

— Cai Guanghua

Have you all noticed two important questions regarding crystal radios? (1) Which crystal is most effective? (2) Why do crystal detectors use crystals?

Regarding the answer to the first question, we have finally made some progress. The crystals we commonly use are roughly lead sulfide (Galena), silicon (Silicon), iron pyrite (Iron Pyrite), and molybdenum (Molybdenum). Recent discoveries suggest that the combination of copper and copper oxide is most effective. In short, until a more effective crystal is discovered, we will tentatively consider the last one as the most complete answer today.

As for the second question, we cannot provide a fully satisfactory explanation at this time; they are all just speculations. According to Dr. W. H. Eccles of England, when current passes through the detector, a thermoelectric effect occurs on the crystal. This electricity itself has a detection effect. The editor of Physical Review, R. E. Goddard, believes this explanation is more reasonable.

However, the general opinion is that crystal detection is entirely based on "surface work." "Surface work" means that when the crystal comes into contact with the metal needle, the electron evaporation on their surfaces is different. The contact point naturally creates different resistances, which gives the crystal a single-transmission property. Therefore, the crystal has the effect of detection.

How to Build a Crystal Radio 155

— Zhu Ziyuan

This crystal radio, when tested in our Songjiang, had excellent results. During the day, it can receive a 100-watt Shanghai station, and at night, a 50-watt station is also very clear. The circuit is shown on the left. Now, the main components are listed below.

CC1 is a 0.0005 microfarad variable capacitor, C2 is a 0.002 microfarad fixed capacitor, D is a fixed crystal, T is an earpiece, A is an antenna, G is a ground wire. The construction of L and L1 is as follows: Use two spiderweb boards, each wound with 60 turns of No. 24 double-cotton covered wire (winding by changing direction every two pins, i.e., alternating two above and two below), with a tap every ten turns, totaling seven taps including both ends. The primary L connects to six tap nails, with its starting end connected to the moving plate of the variable capacitor C, and the tap key connected to the ground wire GC. The fixed plate of C connects to the antenna A1. The secondary L1 connects to five tap nails, with the starting and ending ends connected to the fixed and moving plates of the variable capacitor C1, and the tap key connected to one end of the fixed crystal D. One end of the earpiece T connects to the other end of the fixed crystal, and the other end connects to the moving plate of C1. The bypass capacitor C2 can be connected in parallel across the two terminals of the earpiece. L and L1 are mounted on a movable push-pull frame, which can increase or decrease the distance between the two coils. All components can be mounted on a piece of bakelite. Figure A below shows the top view, and Figure B shows the arrangement on the front of the bakelite. The components used are shown in the following table:

Two 0.0005 microfarad variable capacitors

Two 3-inch diameter degree dials

Two spiderweb boards

One push-pull coil frame (with knob)

Eleven tap nails

Two tap keys

One set of fixed crystal with holder

One 0.002 microfarad fixed capacitor

One earpiece

Approximately 35 yards of No. 24 double-cotton covered wire

Four binding posts

One piece each of bakelite and wooden base

Antenna and ground wire and insulators, etc.

Troubleshooting and Repair of Crystal Radios Jiancun 156

Since crystal radios are simple in construction and use few components, the occurrence of their faults is not as complicated as that of vacuum tube radios. Moreover, the causes of their faults are also easy to find. Once the source of the problem is clear, the repair method is as easy as turning one's hand. Here, the common problems of crystal radios, their sources, and their repair methods are listed below for reference.

(1) The sound gradually becomes faint: This common problem has four sources:

(1) The sensitivity of the crystal detector is reduced: Although there are various methods for testing the quality of a crystal, if you want to test whether the sensitivity of the original crystal is reduced, simply replace it with a new crystal with higher sensitivity to test. Replacing the new crystal and testing it can solve the problem. If the sound is still gradually faint after testing with a new crystal, then the source of the problem is not in the crystal detector. If the sound is loud, then the source of the problem must be in the crystal.

(2) The sensitivity of the earpiece is reduced: This problem is often caused by the weakening of the magnet inside the earpiece and the poor insulation of the earpiece wiring.

(Detection method) Replace the earpiece to test it and remove the earpiece to test its insulation.

(Remedy) Remove the magnet to strengthen it, but this remedy is not easy for ordinary people to implement. You can take it to a repair company and ask them to repair it.

(3) The operation of the coil suddenly becomes poor: The sensitivity decreases due to humidity, etc.

(Detection method) Remove the suspicious coil and replace it with a new coil to test it.

(Remedy) Dry it in the sun.

(4) The sensitivity of the variable capacitor is reduced: The insulation is poor due to dust, humidity, etc.

(Detection method) Replace the capacitor to test it.

(Remedy) Remove the dust and dry it.

(2) The sound suddenly becomes faint:

(1) The sensitivity of the crystal detector suddenly decreases: When the crystal is hit too hard, or when it is electrically shocked by lightning, its sensitivity suddenly decreases.

(Detection method) Compare it with a new crystal.

(Remedy) Replace it with one that is more sensitive.

(2) The antenna touches trees or other objects, or the wire is broken: (Detection method) Investigate whether the antenna is touching trees or other objects, or whether the wire is broken.

(Remedy) Repair the short circuit and broken wire in the antenna.

(3) The ground wire is broken:

(Detection method) Investigate the ground wire, or temporarily make another ground connection to test it.

(Remedy) Connect the broken part of the wire.

Outstanding Crystal Radio 157

— Wei Xinsu

An ideal crystal radio must have the largest possible volume and sharp selectivity. The circuit in the attached diagram is not far from meeting the above conditions. If this circuit is installed in a place in this city where broadcasting stations are densely packed, it can truly reveal its characteristic of sharp selectivity, without weakening the volume. Sitting in a chair, placing the earpiece of this crystal radio on a desk, we can still hear its sound from afar.

In the diagram, L1 is a honeycomb coil. The primary is wound with 80 turns of No. 28 enameled wire on a 4-inch diameter cylinder. The secondary is wound with the same wire and number of turns on a 2-inch diameter cylinder. L2 is wound with 90 turns of No. 24 enameled wire on a 3-inch diameter cylinder, with a tap drawn from its center to connect to the crystal. L3 is wound with 48 turns of No. 28 enameled wire on a 1-inch diameter cylinder. This coil is related to the selectivity of the entire machine. It is best to pull out several taps for adjustment. C1 and C2 are two 0.00035 mf variable capacitors. These two capacitors can also be coaxial. C3 is a 0.001 mf variable capacitor, which is used to adjust the antenna.

Small Experience

Homemade Crystal Method 158

— Pao

Crystals can be homemade, the method is very simple, and the effectiveness of the manufactured crystals is also good. The method is as follows: Take a small amount of sulfur and lead, with a weight ratio of about six parts lead to one part sulfur, mix them thoroughly, and place them in a dry test tube, and then plug it to isolate it from the outside air. Then heat the sulfur and lead with an alcohol lamp or charcoal stove, and after the reaction is complete, let it cool, and then find a way to take it out of the test tube. The product manufactured in this way can be used for crystal detection. If you want to make the effect even better, you can put this manufactured product in a high-temperature-resistant container, such as a hard test tube or porcelain, and then plug it to isolate it from the outside air. Then heat it on a gas lamp or a fierce charcoal fire to liquefy it, and then cool it, and you will get a very good crystal. This is the artificial galena.

Substitutes for Crystal Cups and Crystal Installation Methods 159

Crystal cups can be replaced by the tin lid on ordinary toothpaste tubes, or the small dish on the back of a hunter's bullet cartridge that holds the primer.

When the crystal is installed in this substitute crystal cup, first clean the inside, and then pour in melted tin, and then fix the crystal with pliers in the tin. Another wire is passed through the tin to facilitate wiring. In this way, the contact surface of the crystal is very large, which can increase its effectiveness, and it is also easier to install in the circuit.

Details of the First Day of the Conference 163

The second annual meeting of the Chinese Education Society, after holding the opening ceremony at the gymnasium of Central University on the morning of the 25th, the Nanjing elementary and secondary schools and social education institutions and the Nanjing branch hosted all members at the Central Hotel at noon. In addition to the three papers scheduled on the agenda, there was also an English paper brought by the Beijing Municipal Social Affairs Bureau in the morning. Mr. Liu Tingfang was asked to read it first (limited to ten minutes per person). Mr. Liu then read the English paper from Beijing, "Dr. Mareke's Danish Folk High Schools," and added an explanation. He first said that since the change in the farmer-tenant system in Denmark, there have been 1,500 cooperatives, so the Danish countryside is almost surrounded by cooperatives. Ninety percent of all cattle and seventy-six percent of pigs are registered. Then, he summarized the situation of the Danish education system and national development, and the process of implementing popular education. Chairman Zhuang said that the paper given to us by Dr. Mareke in a hurry will be thanked by the board of directors in the future. Then, Tong Runzhi read the paper "General Situation of Junior Middle Schools in China and the Implementation of the Curriculum." The original text has been printed into a thick volume, and Mr. Tong summarized the report. Then, the chairman reported that Pan Wenan was absent due to business, and his paper "Vocational Education and National Defense" has been requested to be read by his representative Chen Zunshan. Then, Mr. Chen presented the main points of the paper: (1) Factories must be transformed, (2) Talents must be cultivated, (3) Resources must be developed, (4) Rural revitalization must be sought. Then, Zheng Tonghe, representing Cheng Langxi, read the paper "Research on the Chinese Academy System." Mr. Zheng briefly stated that the main points of the paper include (1) the origin of the academy, (2) the Song Dynasty academy, (3) the Yuan Dynasty academy, (4) the Ming Dynasty academy, (5) the Qing Dynasty academy, (6) the abolition of the academy. He also connected and said that the academy first had this term in the Tang Dynasty, but at that time it was a library nature, not teaching students. During the chaos of the Five Dynasties, because scholars generally felt that books were lacking, they had to go to the library-like academy to read books, and the academy's cause was more advanced than before, but it was not yet public. It was gradually made public until the Song Dynasty, with four major academies lecturing. At that time, attention was paid to metaphysics. When the Mongols entered and ruled China during the Yuan Dynasty, the academy system was even better than the Song Dynasty, and attention was also paid to metaphysics. In the early Ming Dynasty, it did not receive much attention, and then it was revived by Wang Yangming's lectures. In the Qing Dynasty, even more special attention was paid to the academy, and academies were established in various provinces, prefectures, and counties. Students who were admitted also received subsidies, which were divided into three types: children, students, and special students. The oldest was over seventy years old, and the youngest was nine years old, with a wide difference. At that time, they were roughly divided into metaphysics, imperial examination, essays, and rhetoric. It was a very prosperous time. During the time of Wei Zhongxian, the academy was destroyed. It was not restored until Wei's death. Until the Guangxu period of the late Qing Dynasty, after the Sino-Japanese War, due to the comparison between China and foreign countries, it was felt that it was not suitable for the needs. Therefore, schools were changed in the 29th year of Guangxu, and the academy system was abolished. Then, the chairman reported that the reading of the papers had been completed, and it was time to start discussing the methods for carrying out the research work of the society, and reported that the board of directors had decided yesterday to submit to the conference the "Plan for Carrying Out the Research Work of the Society," in which the following special topics were proposed: (1) the issue of teacher training, (2) the issue of the realization of compulsory education, (3) the organization and powers of the Education Bureau, (4) the pros and cons of the examination system, (5) the difficulties in the implementation of the new curriculum standards for elementary and secondary schools, (6) the direction and curriculum of university education departments, (7) the nature of people's schools, (8) the implementation of productive education, (9) the review of children's books. Please discuss. Zheng Xiaocang, Ou Yuanhuai, Liu Tingfang, Shao Shulong, and other members all expressed their opinions. First, according to the method of the "Plan for Carrying Out the Research Work of the Society" submitted to the society by the board of directors yesterday, ((1) The annual meeting will decide on research topics, and a committee will be appointed to be responsible for carrying out the research, and each branch will be asked to assist, (2) Introduce educational institutions for experimental research, (3) Solicit individual research from each member)), was passed one by one. Then, the members proposed seven more special topics, adding up to sixteen topics with the nine topics proposed by the board of directors. Then, after the nine topics, (10) the issue of the central thought of Chinese education, (11) rural education, (12) education and national defense, (13) the policy of studying abroad, (14) the future of graduates and further education, (15) civic education, (16) research issues such as character education were added, and it was decided among the sixteen topics that the next annual meeting would focus on the following three issues: (1) the issue of teacher training, (2) the direction and curriculum of university education departments, (3) the implementation of productive education. The remaining topics will be studied as a supplement, depending on the time and personal interests, but they are not specified. Those who are deemed to be central, continue to report the congratulatory telegram from the Beiping branch and the screening of the film by the Ministry of Education in the evening. The Ministry of Education and the Municipal Government will publicly host a banquet tomorrow, and then the meeting adjourned.

School Vacations and Start Dates Should Follow the School Calendar 165

Arbitrary suspension of classes and vacations will be considered a violation of regulations.

Once verified, registration will be revoked as a warning.

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education issued an order yesterday to the registered private primary and secondary schools in this city, stating that the school opening and closing dates have long been clearly stipulated in the school calendar. However, most private schools act independently, arbitrarily suspending classes and taking vacations, which is a deliberate violation of regulations and a disregard for education. If any school continues to fail to comply with the school calendar in the future, the Bureau will revoke its registration as a warning upon verification. Furthermore, the starting date for the second semester of the 22nd year is February 1st. Primary schools will begin classes on the 3rd of the same month, and middle schools will begin classes on the 5th. All of this is clearly stated in the Bureau's Education Weekly No. 202 and has already been communicated for compliance. All schools should comply and not mislead themselves or others. This order is issued for compliance.

Orders for Schools to Purchase

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education issued an order yesterday to municipal and private registered secondary schools, stating that the Bureau has revised the format of student transfer certificates for secondary schools in this city and the method for issuing them, and previously issued a clear order for everyone to comply. Subsequently, the Affiliated Middle School of Guanghua University submitted a report stating that since the format of the transfer certificate has been stipulated by the Bureau, but the thickness of the paper varies, making it difficult to maintain uniformity, they propose that the Bureau print them on their behalf and that schools purchase them from the Bureau when needed. They also propose that all schools in the city use this format starting from the second semester of the 22nd year to facilitate inspection. They request that the Bureau review and implement this proposal. Based on this, the Bureau finds that the proposed opinions are feasible and should be adopted. The Bureau has now printed and bound the transfer certificates into booklets, each containing one hundred pages, priced at seven dimes per booklet. Schools should prepare a letter with payment and purchase them from the Accounting Division of the Bureau starting from the 29th of this month. From now on, all schools should comply with the previous and current orders when issuing these transfer certificates and follow the specified procedures, except that stamps are not required. Please be informed of this order.

Yesterday's Inspection of the Zhuanqiao Agricultural Education Center

Combining these with the library's existing books, paintings, and publications, there are no fewer than four hundred items. Bank Association Holds General Membership Meeting 170

The Bank Association of this city was initiated and organized by colleagues in the banking industry in Shanghai.

It is an organization dedicated to the study of academics by colleagues in the banking industry. Since its establishment on December 9, 1932, its affairs have been flourishing. In addition to publishing journals as research materials for its members, the association has also held many academic lectures, all given by prominent figures in the Shanghai economic community. The audience at each lecture has been very enthusiastic. Therefore, although it has only been established for one year, its achievements are remarkable and can be considered a modern cultural organization. The association held a regular membership meeting at the YMCA Auditorium on Sichuan Road at 5 PM on the 26th of this month. Chairman Xu Xinliu presided over the meeting, and after the rituals were performed, the chairman gave an opening speech, briefly stating that the Bank Association had been established for one year since December 1932, and its affairs had been able to proceed thanks to the cooperation of all members. He also compared the Bank Association with other academic research organizations. After the speech, Mao Xiaxuan, the representative of the Municipal Party Department, gave a speech. Then, Tang Boyuan, the secretary, reported on the progress of the association's affairs, Wang Zhixin reported on the papers submitted by members, and Jin Lvqin reported on the results of the review of the members' proposals. The meeting adjourned at 7:30 PM.

Detailed Record of the Education and Physical Education Committee Meeting 179

Regarding the proposal to participate in the upcoming Far Eastern Games

Budgeted expenses: 90,000. Chief Delegate: Wang Zhengting

Estimated number of athletes: 125 to 150

Continuing to hold the summer physical education class in Qingdao this year

The Education Ministry's Physical Education Committee held its tenth regular meeting at the Ministry of Education from 2:00 PM to 9:00 PM on the 25th. Committee members Chu Minyi, Zhang Zhijiang, Hao Gengsheng, Yuan Dunli, Wu Yunrui, Cheng Dengke, and Shen Siliang attended, as well as observers Zhang Jiong, Zhang Xinfu, Guan Songsheng, Chen Yingmei, Peng Baichuan, Wu Cheng, etc. Chairman Hao Gengsheng reported and discussed the following matters:

A. Reports (1) Unresolved Matters from the First Committee Meeting: 1. The Ministry had previously sent letters of appointment to Wu Yunrui and others to serve on the Education Ministry Physical Education Committee's curriculum discussion committee for all levels of schools. Because the curriculum standards were recently announced, meetings have not been convened for a long time. (Resolution) This case will be merged with the discussion cases for resolution. The work in this case has already been carried out separately by this Ministry and there is no need to convene a meeting again. 2. The National Central Physical Education College case was submitted to the Executive Yuan meeting for the Education and Finance Ministries to jointly discuss with Minister He Jingzhi to handle this case. The second plenary meeting resolved to co-organize the college with the Training Directorate. Subsequently, Committee Member Zhang Jiong negotiated, but cooperation was not possible due to differing natures. The ninth regular meeting resolved to have Committee Members Zhang and Hao develop alternative plans. (Resolution) To be merged with Discussion Case 8 for resolution. Chu Minyi was added to the committee to work with Committee Members Hao and Zhang to develop plans. 3. The second plenary meeting resolved to imitate the operation of the summer physical education training class during the summer of the 23rd year of the Republic. The personnel responsible for preparation and the operating principles of this case have not yet been determined. (Resolution) To be discussed in conjunction with Discussion Case 12. 4. Regarding the implementation of physical fitness standard testing, the materials have been printed and sent to the committee members for their opinions. However, most committee members have not returned them, so it has not yet been carried out. 5. The first plenary meeting resolved to create a method and standard for physical education performance assessment. Because the committee members have not yet determined a method, it has not been carried out. 6. The first plenary meeting resolved to define the scope of women's physical education programs and assigned it to the Physical Education Performance Assessment Method and Standard Research Committee. Currently, this case has not yet determined a method. 7. The third regular meeting resolved to draft detailed curricula and standards for the training of physical education talent, and nominated Committee Members Chu, Zhang, and Huang to draft them. This case has not yet been carried out. (Resolution: The above four items will be discussed in conjunction with Discussion Case 13). 8. The third regular meeting resolved to have Committee Members Zhang and Huang jointly draft regulations for the registration and encouragement of physical education organizations. Because Committee Members Zhang and Huang have not yet drafted and submitted them to the meeting, it has not yet been carried out. (Resolution: Committee Member Hao Gengsheng was added to the committee to jointly draft them). 9. The seventh regular meeting passed that hereafter, all kinds of sports rules and training methods used in the Chinese sports community should be standardized by the regulations of this committee, and other works or translations must also be reviewed by this committee. It was found that many committee members have other tasks, and compiling regulations and reviewing publications takes a lot of time. This committee has not specified concrete measures, so it has not been carried out smoothly. It was resolved that the Ministry should issue a notice to the whole country that hereafter, national martial arts competitions should adopt the rules stipulated by the Central National Martial Arts Hall, and other competitions should use the regulations stipulated by the National Physical Education Advancement Association as the standard. Physical education publications will be temporarily reviewed by this committee. (2) List of Committee Members: Chu Minyi, Zhang Zhijiang, Yuan Dunli, Hao Gengsheng, Wu Yunrui, Shen Siliang, Cheng Dengke (Above are Standing Committee Members); Zhang Xinfu, Huang Liming, Wang Zhengting, Zhang Boling, Ma Liang, Xu Zhiyi, Guan Songsheng, Wu Cheng, Xu Minhui (Chen Yingmei, Ma Yuehan, Zhang Huilan, Gao Xiwei), (3) Committee Member Hao reported on the inspection of the Shanghai Physical Education School.

B. Various Proposals (1) How should the various unresolved cases decided by the first committee meeting be handled separately? (2) There should be a regulation on sports athletes in schools at all levels nationwide (Proposed by Wu Yunrui). (3) The Education Association of Xiangxiang County, Hunan Province, submitted a request to promote public water sports competitions. The Ministry submitted it for discussion. (4) Please stipulate the method for purchasing physical education books and magazines from various countries (Proposed by Wu Yunrui and Hao Gengsheng). (5) The curriculum of junior and senior primary schools is too heavy, how should it be reduced to avoid hindering the health of young people? (Same as above) (6) Stipulate the method for the examination of physical education teachers in primary and secondary schools and implement it as soon as possible (Yuan Dunli). (7) Stipulate the method for further education of physical education teachers in primary and secondary schools (Proposed by Yuan Dunli).

(8) Establishing a National Sports University (Proposed by Cheng Dengke and Wu Cheng). (9) Improving private physical education schools (Same as above). (10) Unifying the national (martial arts) to eliminate factions and compile teaching materials for all levels of application (Same as above). (11) Unifying the national school physical education organization system (Same as above). (12) Opening a national summer physical education training class (Same as above). (13) Implementing national physical education medals and certificates for men, women, children, youth, adults, and military police (Same as above). (14) Preparing to attend the next World Games as soon as possible (Same as above). (15) Revising Article 15, Clause 5 of the tennis competition rules and discussing the length of residence of athletes representing units and the appropriate season for tennis matches (Proposed by Ling Chen Yingmei). (16) Participating in the Far Eastern Games. Committee Member Shen Siliang reported: (1) The Far Eastern Games will be held in Manila, Little Luzon, from May 12th to 19th of this year. There will be nine championship events and five demonstration events. China intends to participate in all championship events. The estimated number of athletes is 125 to 150, with expenses of 90,000 yuan. (2) The participating units are China, Japan, the Philippines, and India. The rumor that the puppet state is participating has been formally denied. (3) The method of selecting athletes is being drafted. In addition to being handled separately by the National Physical Education Advancement Association, this committee will send letters to the physical education committees and physical education advancement associations in various regions to carefully assist in handling. (4) The Advancement Association has decided that Wang Zhengting will be the chief representative, and the government should also send representatives to participate. The number of people in the delegation is set at three. (17) Encouraging domestically produced sports products, regaining rights and interests, in order to seek popularity. (18) Please issue an order from the Ministry to schools and physical education institutions nationwide to use domestic products as much as possible. The resolution was passed by merging the items. (19) It was agreed that the Association and the Social Affairs Bureau would hold the second Beijing City shuttlecock kicking competition in March.

C. Resolved Cases The following discussion items were resolved as follows: Case 2: Yuan Dunli, Wu Yunrui, Cheng Dengke, and Chen Yingmei were nominated to summarize the opinions expressed by the committee members and revise the original draft for discussion at the next meeting. Case 3: Accepted in principle, the committee will send a letter to the association to draft a method, and Committee Members Hao Gengsheng, Wu Yunrui, and Cheng Dengke will be responsible for review. Case 4: Please ask the Ministry of Education's library to purchase as many physical education books from various countries as possible, and the committee members will open book and newspaper lists and submit them to the meeting. Case 5: It is recommended that the Ministry of Education investigate the facts and handle them as appropriate. Case 6: Please ask the Ministry of Education to quickly stipulate the examination method. Case 7: Merged with Case 12 for discussion. Case 8: Merged with Case 1 for discussion. Case 9: After Committee Member Hao investigates the private physical education schools in various regions and makes a formal report, it will be submitted to the meeting for discussion. Case 10: Passed according to the original method proposed, and a letter will be sent to the Central National Martial Arts Hall for reference and handling. Case 11: To be discussed after Committee Member Hao inspects the actual situation. Case 12: Resolved (1) to be held in Qingdao this year, (2) Wu Cheng, Yuan Dunli, and Wu Yunrui were nominated to draft detailed methods for running summer classes and continuing education for physical education teachers, and submit them to the next meeting for discussion. Case 13: This case is merged with Case 1 and Reports 4, 5, 6, and 7. Committee Members Wu Yunrui, Wu Cheng, Cheng Dengke, Yuan Dunli, and Chen Yingmei were nominated to draft detailed methods, and Committee Member Wu will convene them. Case 14: It was decided to participate according to the method proposed by Committee Member Shen Siliang, and the National Physical Education Advancement Association was asked to plan and handle it. Case 15: To be submitted to the preparatory meeting for the next National Games for discussion.

Gold Standard Price Continues to Rise 182

Silver Price and Exchange Rate Continue to Fall and Then Rise Eight Yuan and Four Jiao

The gold market continued to rise yesterday. The situation throughout the day was quite volatile, but the underlying trend was strong, and the outlook is still the same. In the early morning, overseas silver markets in the UK and the US both fell, and the deferred silver price on the Five Metals Exchange fell by 4 to 5%. The exchange rate continued to narrow. London gold fell by nine pence, US cotton was unchanged, stocks fell slightly, and US wheat fell by 1.375 points. The wool market opened and rose to 13 yuan, and major players entered the market, pushing the price closer to the 20 yuan mark. After the opening, the situation seemed tired due to banks' appetite becoming congested, but the price fluctuated. When Sassoon came to supply US dollars, the exchange market hardened and fell, but banks took the opportunity to buy at low prices and the price rose again. Foreign telegrams reported slight purchases of silver. The Guangbang sold contracts, and the lower reaches were active. Later, because the banks' appetite was stagnant, the price fluctuated again. When the banks seized the opportunity to buy cheaply, the dealers sought to close their positions but failed, and the gold market strengthened for a while. It was rumored in the market that the US silver market had reported a significant drop in the night market. However, a Reuters telegram from Washington brought news of the Senate's debate on the currency bill, which had little impact, but people thought it was unfavorable, and the exchange market remained loose. At noon, it was still declining. The later market was initially flat and then firm, which was due to the dealers continuing to close their positions and the banks' appetite occasionally appearing stagnant. Major players such as Dachangxiang have now gone long by more than 1,000 taels, Qianchangxiang has added more than 1,000 taels, Yuan Maoyong covered short positions by 1,000 taels, while Hengyu added short positions. The "cooked red" price was 1,100 yuan. The day's market conditions are recorded below:

The morning opening was 718.5 yuan, up 9 yuan from the previous close. The price of goods opened at 8 yuan. The exchange market opened with near-term selling prices of 1 shilling, 3 pence, 9375 for the British exchange and 33.9375 yuan for the US exchange. Mitsui sold April US dollars at 3.75, Yuan Maoyong and Yongfeng sold, falling to 6.5 yuan. It was expected that HSBC would list the British exchange at a reduction of 125 and the US exchange at a reduction of 375. Qianchangxiang, Dafa Yong, and others came in, rising to 7.8 yuan. After entering, Mitsui bought February US dollars at 125 and sold April at 375. The gold market situation was uncertain. Later, the banks' appetite became congested, and Sassoon also sold. The US dollar domestic market hardened. Zhifeng Yong, Yuan Maoyong, Yiyu, Dakang, Hengtai, Yida, Yongfu Yu, and others sold contracts one after another, falling to 4.2 yuan. Dafa Yong, Hengyu, Yuanchang Yong, Zhaofeng Chang, Yuan Maoyong, and others took the opportunity to buy at low prices. April US dollars were difficult to close at half a yuan, and the price rose to 6.8 yuan. McGill still sold April US dollars at 4.375 and May at 5.625. The situation continued to deteriorate. Later, Tianfeng, Qianchangxiang, Shengda Shunli, Yida Yong, and others came to sell contracts, and the news was unfavorable, retreating to within 5 yuan. However, there were quite a few people taking the opportunity to cover at low prices, and people's hearts were uncertain. Zhengjin bought April US dollars at half a yuan, and February at 1.75. Yuankangxiang and Yuan Maoyong Zhentai handed in contracts one after another, and the price rose to 7.1 yuan. However, this price was difficult to sell. The Dalian gang limited the market to sell but failed, and the price fell. Daxing Yong, Hengyu, and Guangbang successively unloaded their hands. Wahbi sold April US dollars at 4.375, HSBC sold May at 625, and then retreated to 4.1 yuan. Yuan Maoyong and Zhengchang entered contracts, and the price rose again to 5.4 yuan. The East Asia and Wahbi sold April US dollars at half a yuan, Zhengchang suddenly came out at 4 yuan, and the price of goods was handed in. The noon close was 714.9 yuan, and the price of goods was snapped up at 4.8 yuan.

The afternoon opening was 715 yuan, with the same price for goods. Zhengjin sold April

New Standards for Yarn Futures Under Preparation 196

The standard yarn of the Chinese Merchants Yarn and Cloth Exchange has been the 16-count Ren Zhong yarn since it began trading on July 1, 1921. At the same time, Japanese yarn could also be used for delivery. After the May 30th Incident in 1925, the grading of Japanese yarn was removed, and only Chinese yarn was used as the standard. 10-count coarse yarn and 20-count fine yarn were both added for delivery. In 1929, the Indian merchant Qiao Zhifu, a speculator, organized a bull company, purchasing 60,000 bales of March standard yarn and vigorously squeezing the shorts, resulting in a major upheaval. Many sellers found the rapid price increases unsustainable, leading to significant losses and bankruptcies. The highest price reached 183 taels (at that time, the price was quoted in Shanghai 98-regulation yuan). As a result, the shorts lost a total of 2 million taels. Having suffered this major disaster, yarn merchants requested a revision of the standard scope, adopting a broader approach that included all Chinese yarn factories nationwide in the grading system. Yarn produced by factories in Hankou, Tianjin, Wuxi, Changzhou, Taicang, Nantong, and other places was included in the grading table. During the January 28th Shanghai Incident the year before last, Shanghai factories suspended operations for three months, and the exchange also suspended trading. With the evolution of the times, the 20-count fine yarn Ren Zhong was changed to the standard, which was an evolution in the history of standards. Subsequently, on October 16th of last year, the National Economic Committee established the Cotton Industry Control Association, which first attempted to maintain yarn prices. However, this has not been effective, primarily because of rural bankruptcy, financial exhaustion, sluggish yarn sales, and increasing inventories. Coupled with the global cotton industry's slump, market prices have been difficult to stabilize. According to rumors in the market, a certain large factory has been continuously delivering yarn into the exchange's warehouses, with over 20,000 bales of yarn such as Dragon Boat, Caihua, and Ren Zhong. The quality of this cotton yarn is relatively poor, which has depressed market prices. As a result, there have been calls for reform of the standard brand, and the May and June standard yarn futures have been suspended from trading. It is also said that a meeting was held on the 8th of this month to discuss changing the standard to 20-count Golden Chicken yarn. However, some brokers opposed this, so it has not been officially announced and implemented. Further investigation will be conducted and reported.

Free Talk

"Send to See" and "Bring to See" 220

— Yuan Gu

It is said that Eastern and Western cultures are getting closer day by day, which is a gratifying thing. This should be attributed to the steamships, trains, airplanes, and the like invented by foreign devils! As well as the Suez Canal they opened and the Siberian Railway they built. We, with the demeanor of a great nation, the style of an emperor, and the temper of a young master, are taking them all for our enjoyment. What a cause for celebration!

But in culture, we are also broad-minded to the point of indifference! The Japanese have appropriated our writing, the Americans have learned mahjong, and it is said that the French have even learned our cooking. Recently, the Haikyunberg Circus, which caused a sensation in Shanghai, also has people from our country wielding guns and performing. Our culture will soon assimilate the world! What a cause for celebration! But, it’s all up to them!

Let's talk about a "master" in our country who is greatly admired by foreigners. He brought a large batch of paintings, including works by Wu Changshuo, Chen Shizeng, Zhao Zhiqian, and others, to conquer the German art scene. This person had traveled abroad twice, learned that kind of oily tongue, and returned to submit a memorial to the Ministry of Education, which is truly a masterpiece even more lasting than his works of art. Among them, he stated that Europeans worshipped his works without exception, truly placing him high in the heavens! And the great and small artists of Europe in the past all wished they could dig themselves out of the ground to marvel at his works. Perhaps it is the inevitable nature of officials praising each other! But we don't care about it. Even if this person's art conquers the whole world! But here we want to ask, these paintings of modern Easterners have been "sent to see," and perhaps a few have been sold. But are there any paintings by great modern German writers that have been "brought to see"? In principle, the German Ministry of Education should promptly dispatch officials to take many famous paintings from the museum and send them to Shanghai for an exhibition to thank them for this respect. But this, according to people who know the situation of German art, is absolutely impossible for the Germans.

In fact, this is also a matter of no great importance. Eastern and Western art are absolutely incompatible. The two cultures may be close in a thousand years. But we will always offer ourselves, to be enjoyed, used, and pleased by the strong. Just as why agricultural nations make many dried vegetables and store dried fish and meat to guard against nomadic peoples coming and plundering everything, leaving them with no food. At this time, although Germany is in turmoil, it is still a time of "people's well-being and abundant resources," enough to "attract" Eastern art, like the Han Dynasty's "attraction" of ostriches and grapes. And a few rascals, after selling themselves into poverty and becoming destitute, want to obtain approval because of the little things hidden in their homes. The weaker a nation becomes, the more "ingenious" the things it does, and the closer it gets to extinction! If it continues to be "ingenious," it will reach the point where there is no need to "send to see." At that time, there will probably be no art at all.

The Current State of the Literary World 221

— Gu Yuan

This era is somewhat unique: not only are there many strange political phenomena, but also in the literary world, all kinds of monstrous and demonic things emerge endlessly.

Just as the great officials and gentlemen use petty sycophants as a stepping stone to advancement, so too do writers and scholars shout and clamor, using their fellow travelers as stepping stones to climb upwards. When they are shouting and clamoring, they conceal their inherent flaws – especially past shortcomings – in order to win the sympathy of readers.

When they are seeking sympathy and trying to win over the masses, they are passionate, progressive, and appear on the literary scene with a brand-new face. They attack everything old; they want to destroy and demolish the old foundations and create a new one; they are exhibiting

the fearless spirit of a revolutionary.

All of this is the same as a newly emerged political commentator.

They are noticed by the masses and loved by the reading public; even the old forces regard them as leaders and representatives of the new generation and secretly send them "autumn waves" of flirtation.

At this time, they have an unshakeable position in society, and they no longer need the support of young people. Their influence extends into the circles of the old forces. They become members of the old forces; the old forces welcome the newly joined powerful elements; and they are also eager to support everything old – they want to climb higher, stepping on a different kind of ladder.

They completely become another kind of person, completely revealing their original hideous face; they no longer shout, they no longer clamor, and instead regard the passionate shouts of others as disturbing their peaceful life. They know all the secrets of the old and new literary worlds; they know how to cater to the old forces in order to create a new position for themselves; at the same time, they also know how to lure later arrivals and how to deceive their eyes and ears. They are "those who have been there"; even more terrifying than all the old forces, they are "those who have been there" who can lead a group of blind young people down a dead end.

Their boldness, their ability to flatter, their ability to create their own new positions, and even their shamelessness, are all things that the old forces do not possess. Confucius killed the Lu grandee Shaozheng Mao, saying: "There are five great evils in the world, and theft is not among them. A mind that is rebellious and dangerous, conduct that is perverse and obstinate, words that are deceitful and clever, a memory that is broad and remembers ugliness, and compliance with what is wrong and glamorous. Shaozheng Mao possesses all of these, and cannot be eliminated." This precisely describes their crimes!

Whenever a new force rises in the literary world, there will always be such people; the so-called people who achieve great fame and become pillars of the literary world, such as Wang Shizhen, Chen Meigong, Yuan Zicai, etc., are all like this, and today there are even more.

From old-style warlords to new-style gangsters, all regard them as people of the same kind, like licorice root in medicine, suitable for everything; and they are "universally accepted" and blend together like water and milk.

The old forces secretly laugh and are pleased: "To catch the bandits, you must first catch the king. Now, the newly emerging king is caught in our hands; they ultimately cannot escape our grasp. Who knew they would be so docile and understand people's intentions!" And having some new figures interspersed among them is enough to show that they are "new." – And this camouflage allows them to remain at peace without even transforming.

Those who have advanced into the circles of the old forces also secretly laugh and are pleased: "It was only ever a stepping stone to advancement. Why keep the bridge after crossing the river?" Aiding the oppressive and helping the wicked, how they bolster and augment the power of the old forces!

Originally, there were two distinctly separate boundaries: to advance or retreat, to come to the new or to go to the old. You are not allowed to hesitate, you are not allowed to waver, you are not allowed to equivocate in between. But now the battle lines are blurred; they are leading a portion of the youth to compromise with and surrender to the old forces; while at the same time, they still solemnly put on a front of new leaders. Their reading public has not yet fully realized their despicable behavior; their masses still retain some faith in them; they sell out their positions as new leaders, but at the same time, they use the old forces to consolidate their positions.

This influence is bad enough: a portion of the younger people, shocked by their past shouts and cries, almost to the point of superstition, excessively believe them, and then innocently begin to have doubts and waver about the new battle lines. Writing ancient-style regulated verse, writing lyrics and composing melodies, and even learning to carve seals and practice calligraphy – everything has returned to the bustling atmosphere of the Guangxu and Xuantong eras and the early Republic. How heartbreaking it is to talk about!

Who would have thought that things would change so quickly! From overthrowing old poetry and promoting new poetry, they turn around and start writing "lyrics" again; from saying that they would throw away all old Chinese books, it is not long before they are advocating writing fu! They advocate writing classical Chinese prose and reading more old books, saying that they want to gain something from old books.

If we were to talk about revolutionary "opportunists," then this group of writers and scholars are truly "opportunists."

They are also the same as political opportunists: they use their fellow travelers as a stepping stone to advancement. Once they step onto the highest level of the ladder, they immediately abandon them.

Today, the ones who advocate that university students should write classical Chinese prose in universities are not the ones who came from the New Culture Movement; today, the ones who say that they want to fill in lyrics and read ancient books are not the ones who gained the upper hand in the New Literature trend.

The true faces of the opportunists are finally hideously revealed.

Thus, the entire battle line is in disarray; everyone has forgotten what kind of crimes the Black Curtain Faction left behind; and they then mix into the new ranks, and the so-called "new people" no longer shout and no longer attack the old forces, and instead become "hangers-on" in the camps of those they previously regarded as enemies.

The new and the old are mixed together, the new and the old are compromising, and the battle lines that opposed them have been removed.

The world is at peace; it has returned to the bustling situation of the Guangxu, Xuantong, and early Republic eras.

But is the world really at peace?

Another new battle line, a new barrier, is being erected.

A group of past new people have been swallowed up by the circles of the old forces! But they will eventually walk the same path to destruction as the old forces!

Emperor Addiction 222

— Yu Shixia

Some say that Puyi is dreaming of being emperor again. I, however, think that he is not dreaming of being emperor, but rather indulging in an emperor addiction; he is almost worse than Shi Jingtang, and is like Zhang Bangchang and Liu Yu. Zhang Bangchang's puppet state lasted only forty-odd days, and Liu Yu's puppet state lasted only seven years. Puyi's puppet state, even if it is longer than Zhang Bangchang's, may not be shorter than Liu Yu's. How long can his self-satisfied theft of the imperial title last? However, like those addicted to opium, who know that it is extremely harmful, but only want to get their fix, and disregard everything to obtain it. Those with an emperor addiction are happy to be an emperor's subject, an emperor's nephew, a child emperor, or a grandson emperor. Even a local emperor or a bandit emperor is acceptable.

During the late years of Wang Mang's dynasty, Gongsun Shu, based in Shu, wanted to become emperor. He dreamt that someone told him, "Eight private strokes, the thread of a child, twelve is the limit." When he awoke, he said to his wife, "Although noble, the reign is short. What shall we do?" His wife replied, "If one hears the Way in the morning, it is acceptable to die in the evening, let alone twelve years?" So he established himself as the Son of Heaven and named his state Chengjia. During the Xiankang era of the Jin dynasty, Li Shou, based in Shu, also wanted to become emperor, and ordered a divination. The diviner said, "He can repeatedly count as the Son of Heaven." His subordinate Ren Diao joyfully said, "One day is enough, let alone several years?" Jie Siming said, "Several years as the Son of Heaven, which is better than a hundred generations as a marquis?" Shou said, "If one hears the Way in the morning, it is acceptable to die in the evening." Ren Hou's words were the best strategy. So he presumptuously took the throne. This is an example of someone indulging in a local emperor addiction.

Also, during the time of Emperor An of the Jin dynasty, Wang Shi gathered a crowd in Mount Tai and declared himself the Taiping Emperor, calling his father the Supreme Emperor, his elder brother the General Who Pacifies the East, and his younger brother the General Who Pacifies the West. Murong Zhen attacked and captured him, and beheaded him in the marketplace. Before his execution, someone asked where his father and brothers were. Shi replied, "The Supreme Emperor is covered in dust abroad. The General Who Pacifies the East and the General Who Pacifies the West were killed by the rebel army. Only I am alone and desolate." His wife angrily said, "You are only in this state because of your mouth! Why do you say that again?" Shi said, "Empress! From below, is there any family that is not broken, any country that is not destroyed?" The executioner struck him with the pommel of his sword. He looked up and said, "I may collapse, but I will never renounce the imperial title!" This is an example of someone indulging in a bandit emperor addiction.

Alas! Shi Jingtang's addiction to being a child emperor and Shi Chonggui's addiction to being a grandson emperor were already ugly enough. But the Southern Song dynasty, from Emperor Xiaozong onwards, shamelessly indulged in a nephew emperor addiction, so why criticize Zhang Bangchang and Liu Yu for indulging in a subject emperor addiction? I just don't know what level Puyi is at now, indulging in his emperor addiction.

Review of "Jealousy" (Continued) 223

— Shi Heng

From here, we can see the evils of the last World War, the waste of human bloodshed and sacrifice. The historical facts are clearly displayed before our eyes: the European War was a war caused by the uneven distribution of spoils by the imperialists, and the people of the participating countries were suffering from

life and weary of the whip of life, hoping for a huge stimulus and encouragement to change their lives, so they were misled by the false slogans of so-called justice and patriotism, exploited, and sent to the front lines of the war. If these people died, they would be blessed, because they would not have the opportunity to taste the more intense new pain of awakening after the war. It is very clear that these people were blind, that this war was an idealess melee, that their sacrifices were of no value, and that after a drunken frenzy, they awoke to see only loss, falling into an abyss of despair that even deprived them of all vitality. Their only hope was to change their lives through that war and create a new path of life, and this ultimately became a dream; and before the war, they were able to support the burden of life, but now, whether mentally or physically, they have become disabled people, still thrown back into the same weary and painful life as before, which is more unbearable than dying on the front lines.

Andre, the middle school teacher in "Jealousy," is a good example of this. Four years of captivity destroyed this man. Although his body is not disabled, we can see the hidden illness in his soul. His wife says that he needs a year of rest, which is too short; he needs a lifetime of rest. But after he returns, he still has to work as a hated middle school teacher, still has to be his wife's husband, and painfully fulfill all the responsibilities of being a person. He cannot bear it. At this time, even the smallest thing can become the cause of the destruction of life, and the suspicion or jealousy of his wife is only an accidental opportunity.

Therefore, it is not very convincing to say that jealousy destroyed this man's happy life, and it is not right to put all the blame on this husband. However, in the event described by the author, the wife is in a passive position. Like her husband, Blanche also spent the same four years in captivity, suffering the same pain. According to the sociologist Rosso's analysis of the psychology of wartime people, these women were as bewitched as the men. Although they could not personally go to the front lines, they encouraged their husbands and welcomed all the soldiers who went to the front lines, because they were also oppressed by the weariness and difficulties of past lives, and they were also hoping for the creation of a new life. But the result of the war only brought harm, and life still went on the old track, and was even more miserable. Therefore, what Blanche, who represents these women, said when she thought of going to America to seek a new way of life, best expresses their general psychology. In this play, although Blanche is written as passive, can she not be in an active position in another play of life? If it is said that becoming active is indeed more common among men than women, is it not because the degree of stimulation and pain that the World War gave them is different? The amount of pain that the war gave them is directly proportional to the power they have to resist the old ways of life.

Look, in the whole play, only Andre's father did not have much disappointment after the war. He also suffered four years of pain, but he has nothing to be dissatisfied with because his son can return, because he is already a seventy-five-year-old man. When Andre expresses his grievances to him, we hear the old man say, "...Oh! Let it go, let's be quiet, you're home. Your woman loves you. Are you still not satisfied? I can guarantee with my head that she has not been unfaithful to you. But even if she has been unfaithful to you, what's the use of making a fuss now? Live a life of contentment for me and don't think about anything else. Everyone has come through such misfortunes." He does not understand his son, and he cannot understand the real reason for Andre's dissatisfaction.

I said at the beginning that, in my opinion, the original title of this book, "Rekindling the Broken Fire," is more expressive of the meaning of this play than "Jealousy," but if the breakdown of the love between the long-separated couple is seen as rekindling the broken fire, that is wrong. Being deceived by the meaningless World War, which made them hope for a new life, and that hope has not been fulfilled, is the real "Rekindling the Broken Fire"!

I have indeed seen this meaning from this play, and this meaning is also fully and truthfully expressed in the play, although the author has not clearly explained it, it is still a profound and good drama. The greatest lesson that this play gives us is that the last World War was a chaotic battle with no benefits, which only added another layer of unbearable pain to the people of Europe, and gave us nothing else. (The End)

Father and Daughter (7) 224

— Jin Yi

"He no longer, longer—am I still alone after I undress him?"

"Yes, he is alone, but he is very happy."

She saw the female guest shake her head sadly, but her own heart gradually became happy because she thought this answer was very appropriate.

"Is that really so?"

The female guest did not dare to fully believe her words. She did not say anything more, only nodding.

"Where did he go tonight?"

"To see a friend, he won't be back until very late."

"Then please tell him that a woman came to see him—tomorrow, tomorrow I can't get away, I can't come again."

"Won't you tell him your name?"

She deliberately asked.

"I think he should remember, and you should too—it's getting late, I think I should go. There are still some things I want to ask, but it's too much trouble for you."

"It's nothing, you can say whatever you want."

"Has he ever mentioned a woman to you?"

"No, he never talks about women."

"Do you know your mother?"

"I don't know, I don't have a mother, I never knew I had a mother."

She suppressed the emotions rising in her chest and deliberately said this indifferently. But she saw the female guest looking at her with bright eyes, as if saying these words:

"You don't not have a mother, the one in front of you is your mother, don't you really know? Come here, child, I know I was wrong. I'm not worthy to be your mother, I haven't given you any motherly love since you were born, now come here, child, let me hug you, kiss you."

She understood these things, but she endured it and did not move, she saw that the female guest's eyes were covered with a thin layer of clear tears. But she deliberately looked away, pretending not to see it.

In the expression of spiritual life, they believe that worldly affairs are like smoke and clouds, and human life is like straw dogs. Therefore, in dealing with things, they adhere to the principle of not contending with others, muddling through, and regard international competition and national survival as something that can be ignored. This is the meaning of what Dai Dongyuan called "Dangers and ease do not linger in the heart, ten thousand bushels of floating clouds pass through the vast sky." Similarly, Britain played this trick in Egypt, and France in Annam. Therefore, the essence of this Asian Student Conference, which "hopes for harmony between Eastern and Western nations," does not lie in opposing civilizations "lacking soul and thought," but in: 1. Using the sweet words of uniting Eastern and Western nations to save the world's civilization from danger to show goodwill to the nations of the Far East, so that Italy, which is in conflict with France in the Mediterranean, can extend its power to the Far East. The unity of Eastern and Western nations has the same practical meaning as "the same script, the same race, co-existence and co-prosperity." 2. Praising the passive national character of Eastern nations, so that Italy, on the day it extends its power to the Far East, can still promote the beauty of "Eastern civilization" without strong resistance, and maintain the "spiritual victory" of Eastern nations.

Maintaining Eastern civilization, cultivating spiritual life, and restoring old morality once stirred up waves in China. Now this call is very weak. This is not because it has already been conquered by Western civilization, which lacks soul and thought. Needless to say, the promotion of maintaining Eastern civilization has been fully adopted in life. Even if the power of Western civilization conquers China again and turns it into a second India or Annam, it doesn't matter. Foreign warships and cannons will never break through the barrier of our "soul," and we will still be "spiritually" victorious!

Naturally, this spiritual victory will also be Mussolini's victory of "unity between Eastern and Western nations" in the future.

After Talking About "Eugenic Laws" 225

— Zhi

Human evolution has reached its highest degree, and the struggle for survival is even more intense and tense. Darwin's great truth of "survival of the fittest" has dominated the entire course of our human race, and "might makes right" has followed it, dominating this world for twenty centuries. Just to savor this ending from the point of view of the preciousness of life, how tragic and bleak it is!

Those who are strong use force to bully the weak, but eugenicists harden their hearts and say that this is the victory of the superior and the elimination of the inferior, and that these weak people have no right to survive in this world, which is even more tragic and bleak!

The world is a place where the strong compete, and everyone wants to compete for strength and hegemony, so wars appear; mobile warfare, engagements, border wars, siege warfare, defensive warfare, annihilation warfare, attrition warfare, air warfare, land warfare, sea warfare, airplanes, tanks, torpedoes... all kinds of strategic weapons have also been invented and applied. This world is full of bleak destruction and brutal killing, and everywhere we can witness the preparation for war and the incitement to war, heroism, patriotism, iron-bloodedism! These nice-sounding terms are often hung on the bodies or mouths of those who are powerful. They hold their fists and carry their guns with self-importance, wanting to show off their skills in this world, which means to carry out a ruthless massacre of the weak, so that they cannot survive in this world.

If humans want to survive, they must be involved in this whirlpool of war. Individuals must prepare to be born from death, and countries must prepare to be defeated by war. When we open our eyes and look at it, isn't this the picture of the world? —The strong sing songs of victory, and the weak chant mournful tunes.

Darwin's theory was originally a very correct theory of biological evolution. Unfortunately, when the theory was applied to social problems, it gave rise to the iron rule of "might makes right," trampling on countless lives, and still trapping mankind in an abyss from which there is no return.

The Berlin telegram reported the other day: "The German government's law 'Eliminating Reproductive Function' will be implemented from January 1 next year. Approximately 400,000 people with hereditary diseases will be subject to this law, especially the disabled..."

. This is naturally based on the principles of eugenicists, with the intention of strengthening the race and strengthening the seed. This contains the explosive potential of war, and the great ambitions of those heroes, patriots, and iron-bloodedists are also revealed in this.

Congratulations 227

— Jian Ren

Because a colleague was getting married, as usual, everyone had to chip in for a gift. But what would be a good gift to give? Wei Jun, who was experienced in the ways of the world, said that it would be best to give money. Because in this day and age, what everyone lacks is "it," and this is more practical than anything else. "Let them buy their own gifts! If they don't need to buy anything, they can use the money as reimbursement for the banquet, wouldn't that be more considerate of friends?" Wei Jun's words won everyone's approval, so many "shares" were wrapped in a large red paper envelope.

The next problem that arose was what words should be written on this red envelope. It had to be neither outdated nor inelegant. Everyone thought for a long time, all smiling without speaking, and I, holding a writing brush in my hand, was a bit embarrassed at this moment. Ping suggested four words: "Dragon and Phoenix Harmonize."

"Too old," Qing said.

"I don't think it's too old, but..." I said.

Qing retorted:

"But what? Say it!"

"I thought of an article about 'Dragon and Phoenix Ideology.' I don't like using those two words, but as for the words 'Harmonize,' I completely agree with them," I said.

"You're talking philosophy, we don't understand at all," Qing said.

"It's better not to understand. Once you understand, it's a bit uncomfortable. Maybe someone won't want to get married. Haha."

"What a wonderful theory is this? Tell us a little, would you?" Jing, who never spoke, wanted to hear the wonderful theory now. "It's a story, no! It's a philosophical conversation. It says that fathers always hope their sons become dragons; they always save money and cut expenses to find phoenixes for their sons. Once the dragon and phoenix wedding cakes are eaten, the sons soon become fathers, but they themselves have not become dragons, so they have to turn around and hope for their own sons. So this author concluded: 'Thousands upon thousands of young people have been harmed by the dragon and phoenix ideology. Their experience is insufficient, their knowledge inadequate, their bodies weak, and their burdens too heavy, damaging all their achievements. Many geniuses are buried and injured because of this, and society suffers a great loss. People still laugh and eat dragon and phoenix cakes, wear clothes with dragon and phoenix patterns, and use utensils with dragon and phoenix patterns, shrouded in an atmosphere of sadness, depression, bewilderment, and haze, advancing step by step with Father Time!' Doesn't this have some reason?"

"Reasonable! Reasonable! This article is more like a speech by Mrs. Sanger!" Wei Jun was quite enlightened.

"I don't agree! I don't believe a person's lack of progress is all because of marriage, and it's all the women's fault!" Qing was standing up for the women!

"Haha! What you say is also reasonable! Do you support 'Dragon and Phoenix Harmonize'?"

"Bah! I think it's old."

Ping then suggested "The Creator's Mischief," but Qing also rejected it because it was a bit inelegant, even though Ping cited many "nationalistic" words, she could not soften Qing's firm denial.

In the end, Wei, who was experienced in the ways of the world, said, wait for me, why bother working on these few words! He snatched the pen and wrote two large characters on the red envelope: "Congratulations." Everyone smiled and agreed without objection. Because these two words are neither new nor old, and are appreciated by both the refined and the vulgar. Wei is indeed a clever and capable person, I thought to myself.

Unexpectedly, Qing then fell silent.

"What else are you dissatisfied with?" Wei asked. "I feel that life is always full of worries. In a person's marriage, what is there to congratulate? For example, Jian's marriage this time is the beginning of his suffering. These two words are just mocking them."

"Haha!" Wei laughed, "Miss Qing is also going to be a philosopher. But young people shouldn't be too serious. Difficulties are always going to be difficult. Let's talk about it when the time comes!"

"You yourself are a 'Let's talk about it when the time comes' philosopher!"

"Hahaha!" Everyone laughed, and Wei said triumphantly, "What a formidable young lady! When shall we 'congratulate' your 'joy'?"

Amateur Mailbox

Employee Food and Lodging Problems Letter Published 228

Editor:

I carefully read "An Employee's Food and Lodging Problems" published in your newspaper's amateur mailbox on the 20th of this month and feel that this problem is not as serious as Mr. Yu and your editor claim. In this day and age, the biggest fear is unemployment. If one has a job paying twenty-two yuan, as long as one "has a plan," there's no need to fear there's no solution.

I have a friend, Mr. Zhang, who has been in Shanghai for over twenty years. Initially, his salary was only fifteen yuan per month, and now it's only a little over forty yuan. His working hours are from 8 am to 6 pm, and the company only provides lunch, the same as Mr. Yu. He has three solutions: (1) Absolutely do not bring family to Shanghai, because this is the most uneconomical. (2) Sometimes rent a garret; sometimes four people rent a room together, with bunk beds. Those sleeping on the top bunk pay one or two yuan per month, and those sleeping on the bottom bunk pay double. (One of the four always knows someone who will rent even to those without families.) (3) Eat a full lunch, glutinous rice and fried dough sticks in the morning, and porridge and pancakes at night. Therefore, his monthly personal expenses used to be only five or six yuan, and now they are only ten yuan.

I don't want to take up too much of your newspaper's space, so I won't say more. We think, with Mr. Zhang's solution, can't everything be resolved! Sincerely, Yang Songqing

Manli's Suicide (8) 229

— Man Zhi

The big fat Mr. Zhang suddenly broke the silence in the room. An expression of great surprise first appeared on his big face, and then he said:

"Didn't the Today's Times report a young man jumping into the Huangpu River? Renjie might be..."

These words certainly attracted attention, but they were immediately refuted by Mr. Huang, who had a small mustache. Mr. Huang said: "That was a superficial student. His will said that he couldn't bear to see China's demise. It's not him."

"Moreover," I added, "Renjie is a man of strong will. He is most opposed to suicide. He says suicide is the act of the weak, a shameful act."

"Isn't he heartbroken? It's common for heartbroken people to commit suicide."

The big fat Mr. Zhang still insisted on his view.

"It depends on what kind of person he is. How can someone like Renjie, a heroic figure with ideas and accomplishments, be compared?"

The small-mustached Mr. Huang refuted again.

The big fat Mr. Zhang nodded, took a puff of his cigarette, and silently acknowledged that this made sense. Everyone was also silent.

Suddenly, Mr. Lei, who had a melon-seed face and a red nose, shouted in a high-pitched voice: "Hey, I was chatting with Renjie a few days ago, and he greatly praised the bravery of the Northeast Volunteer Army, saying that what they were doing was meaningful. Could it be that he joined the Volunteer Army?"

"I've heard him say that too. Maybe that's it!" The big fat Mr. Zhang echoed.

The small-mustached Mr. Huang said with some doubt, "Probably not!"

"Wrong," I denied, "Renjie also scolded those volunteer soldiers for not being organized and unable to succeed."

"That's hard to say. Although he thinks they won't succeed, if he thinks he can succeed by organizing them himself, he might go."

The red-nosed Mr. Lei insisted on his view.

"I think he went to so-and-so. That's more believable," the small-mustached Mr. Huang said, strengthening his words.

"So-and-so?"

"Not necessarily, not necessarily!"

The big fat Mr. Zhang and the red-nosed Mr. Lei both denied it, as if it were their own business.

"I have evidence," the small-mustached Mr. Huang said. "The night before last, in the park, I saw Renjie talking secretly with a man in a cloth robe in the pavilion from a distance. After a while, that man left hurriedly. I went up to him, and Renjie was smiling very happily, looking at the moon in the sky. I called out to him, and his face immediately changed color. He looked back at me in a panic. When he saw clearly that it was me, the first thing he asked was if I had been there for a long time. I said I had just arrived, and then he smiled. That kind of panicked expression showed that he had a secret on his mind. When the person he was talking to left the pavilion, I saw that he was someone from so-and-so, with disheveled hair and unkempt clothes."
